## Overview

Francois Beaufort

**Francois Beaufort** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in the [Honorhall Orphanage](/wiki/Skyrim:Honorhall_Orphanage "Skyrim:Honorhall Orphanage") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). His parents left him at the orphanage around a year prior to the events of the game, and he is waiting for them to return and collect him, as they promised him they would. However, it's likely he was abandoned. He approves of [Aventus Aretino's](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino") plans to summon the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and hopes [Grelod the Kind](/wiki/Skyrim:Grelod_the_Kind "Skyrim:Grelod the Kind") will be killed. Once she is, he cheers with joy along with the other orphans.

During your first visit to the orphanage, Grelod can be heard verbally abusing Francois and his friends, [Runa](/wiki/Skyrim:Runa_Fair-Shield "Skyrim:Runa Fair-Shield"), [Hroar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroar "Skyrim:Hroar"), and [Samuel](/wiki/Skyrim:Samuel "Skyrim:Samuel"):

**Grelod**: *"Those who shirk their duties will get an extra beating. Do I make myself clear?"*
**Orphans**: *"Yes, Grelod."*
**Grelod**: *"And one more thing! I will hear no more talk of adoptions! None of you riff-raff is getting adopted. Ever! Nobody needs you, nobody wants you. That, my darlings, is why you're here. Why you will always be here, until the day you come of age and get thrown into that wide, horrible world. Now, what do you all say?"*
**Orphans**: *"We love you, Grelod. Thank you for your kindness."*
**Grelod**: *"That's better. Now scurry off, my little guttersnipes."*

He then resumes his normal schedule: he gets up at 6am and stays in the orphanage building. He heads to the yard at 10am, playing with the other children for one hour before returning inside. At 3pm he is allowed to eat for one hour, and goes to bed at 10pm.

He wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Shoes"). He carries a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

Before you kill Grelod, he will tell you, *"I do hope mummy and father come to get me soon. Ever since that Aventus boy left, Grelod has been so angry."*, *"My parents dropped me off here a year ago. But they're coming back to get me. They said so."* or *"You look kind of scary. But nobody is scarier than old Grelod."* If [Constance Michel](/wiki/Skyrim:Constance_Michel "Skyrim:Constance Michel") is alive, he will also say, *"Constance Michel says we have to be careful of people we don't know."*

If you have not talked to [Aventus Aretino](/wiki/Skyrim:Aventus_Aretino "Skyrim:Aventus Aretino"), you can ask Francois to tell you more about him: *"Oh, Aventus Aretino. He was sent here when his mother died, but he ran away."* If Grelod is alive, he will continue by saying, *"I heard he went back to his house in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), and is trying to get the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") to come and murder Grelod. That would be so wonderful."* If not, he will instead say, *"I heard he went back to his house in Windhelm, to try and get the Dark Brotherhood to come and murder Grelod. And... he actually pulled it off!"* When asked about Grelod, he will respond, *"Miss Grelod is... well she's a terrible old crone. No person could be that cruel. I think she's part [hagraven](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven "Skyrim:Hagraven"). She only lets us out in the yard once. In the morning. And she just stands there watching us. Like I said. Hagraven."*

He will be overjoyed to see the cruel headmistress die, as he'll exclaim, *"Oh my goodness!"*, *"We love you, Dark Brotherhood! Ha ha ha ha ha!"* or *"Yay!"* Before you return to Aventus, Francois will also express his disbelief: *"I can't believe it! Grelod is dead! She's really dead!"* If you murdered Grelod before going to Aventus, he will comment, *"I do hope mummy and father come to get me soon. Ever since that Aventus boy left, this place has gone mad."*

## Notes

- The name "Francois Beaufort" is more typically Breton than Imperial. The reason for this unusual naming choice is unknown.

Frea

**Frea** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") living in [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village"). She is the daughter of [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider"), the village's shaman, and will replace him after his death. Once you progress far enough into the Dragonborn main questline, you can convince her to be a follower if your [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") is at least 25 (see [this section](#Follower_Dialogue)).

Frea wears [Nordic carved armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Armor "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Boots "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Boots") and [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Carved_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Nordic Carved Gauntlets"), as well as a unique [Skaal amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Amulet "Skyrim:Skaal Amulet") which protects her from [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s influence. She carries two war axes, one [stalhrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_War_Axe "Skyrim:Stalhrim War Axe") and the other [Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_War_Axe "Skyrim:Nordic War Axe"), as well as a [Nordic bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Bow "Skyrim:Nordic Bow") and 12 [Nordic arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Arrow "Skyrim:Nordic Arrow"). She knows the [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration") spells [Ebonyflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebonyflesh "Skyrim:Ebonyflesh") and [Ironflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironflesh "Skyrim:Ironflesh"), and the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spells [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Heal Other](/wiki/Skyrim:Heal_Other "Skyrim:Heal Other").

If you use her as a follower throughout the Main Questline of Dragonborn, she has unique dialogue to environments or certain situations. She also makes comments in response to the context of other NPCs' dialogue.

## Related Quests

- **[The Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak")**: Uncover the source of [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s power in the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak").
- **[The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal")**: Find a way to free the citizens of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village").
- **[The Gardener of Men](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gardener_of_Men "Skyrim:The Gardener of Men")**: Travel to the realm of [Hermaeus Mora](/wiki/Skyrim:Hermaeus_Mora "Skyrim:Hermaeus Mora") to learn the rest of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will").
- **[At the Summit of Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha")**: Confront [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)") at the summit of [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") and defeat him once and for all.
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Quest-Related Events

 "Skyrim:The Temple of Miraak (achievement)")

#### Trouble in Solstheim

*"Oslaf, please!"*

As you arrive in Solstheim, its residents will seem dazed and under the influence of a mysterious force. Most people will vaguely mention a temple and point you to the [Temple of Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Miraak "Skyrim:Temple of Miraak"). As you arrive, you'll find mindless workers building on the temple and Frea shouting at the ensnared workers:

:   *"[Oslaf](/wiki/Skyrim:Oslaf "Skyrim:Oslaf"), please! You must fight against what is controlling you!"*, *"[Ysra](/wiki/Skyrim:Yrsa "Skyrim:Yrsa")*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, can you hear me? Ysra*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, I'm here to help you!"*
:   *"You must leave this place! It is not safe here! We must go back to the village!"*
:   *"You must listen to me! We must leave this place!"*

When she notices you, she'll approach you:

:   *"You there. What brings you to this place? Why are you here?"*
:   **Who are you?**
:   *"I am Frea of the Skaal. I am here to either save my people, or avenge them."*
:   **Save them from what?**
:   *"I am unsure. Something has taken control of most of the people of Solstheim. It makes them forget themselves, and work on these horrible creations that corrupt the [Stones](/wiki/Skyrim:All-Maker_Stones "Skyrim:All-Maker Stones"), the very land itself. My father Storn, our shaman, says Miraak has returned to Solstheim, but that is impossible."*
:   **This Miraak tried to have me killed.**
:   *"Then you and I both have reason to see what lies beneath us. Let us go. There is nothing more I can do here. The Tree Stone and my friends are beyond my help for now. We need to find a way into the temple below."*

You can now ask her a few questions:

:   **What is the [Tree Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Tree_Stone "Skyrim:Tree Stone")?**
:   *"It is an ancient stone of power, a connection to the All-Maker. It represents one of the aspects of nature, a part of the All-Maker's creation. There are other stones around Solstheim. I fear for what has happened to them..."*

:   **You're here by yourself?**
:   *"There are few of us left unaffected by this curse. My father Storn, the shaman, protects them in the village. I fashioned an amulet to guard me against whatever has taken hold of the Skaal, but it is the only one of its kind. If I cannot find a way to save them, there is no hope for our people."*

:   **What do you know about Miraak?**
:   *"His story is as old as Solstheim itself. He served the dragons before their fall from power, as most did. A priest in their order. But unlike most, he turned against them. He made his own path, and his actions cost him dearly. The stories say he sought to claim Solstheim for himself, and the dragons destroyed him for it."*

:   **Tell me of your people, the Skaal.**
:   *"We have lived on Solstheim for many generations. Our people are tied to the land itself. We try to serve the All-Maker, to live in balance with nature, instead of exploiting it as others would."*

When greeted, she'll now express hope:

:   *"If anyone can help us now, it is you."*

When leaving conversation:

:   *"We must find out what is at work here."*

If you learn the first word of [Bend Will](/wiki/Skyrim:Bend_Will "Skyrim:Bend Will") at [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") and cleanse the [Wind Stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Wind_Stone "Skyrim:Wind Stone") before first meeting Frea, Storn will send you to find her. She will still greet you by asking who you are, to which you can tell her Storn sent you:

:   **Storn sent me to find you.**
:   *"I do not understand. Why would he send you, an outsider, to find me when he knows why I have come here? Our people are lost to the madness that infects this island. Perhaps Storn has been lost as well..."*
:   **Relax, everyone is safe.**
:   *"Truly? Thank the All-Maker! But still, this temple stands. The Tree Stone remains tainted. How can we be sure the Skaal will remain free? I can not return to the village until I have found the source of this evil. Will you come with me, further into this accursed temple?"*

The quest will then proceed as normal.

#### Temple of Miraak

*"I do not wish to imagine the kinds of things that happened in this chamber."*

Upon entering the first room of the temple:

:   *"Are you ready to help me now? We should not delay. We should check these rooms for supplies before heading further into the temple. I shall look around. We can proceed when you are ready."*

When she is done searching the rooms, she'll say:

:   *"Take your time. I shall follow when you are ready."*

As you press on and leave the first area of the temple and head to the next chamber, she'll say:

:   *"We must be careful in these ruins. Traps can be anywhere, and there will likely be many. Miraak was trying to take power here, and protect himself in the process."*

As you continue on and find a torture chamber, she'll say:

:   *"I do not wish to imagine the kinds of things that happened in this chamber. Who were the poor souls trapped in these cages? What tortures did they suffer at Miraak's hands? Was it in service to the dragons, or for his own purposes?"*

She'll then look up and say:

:   *"Look up there. I think I see something."*

She'll then walk over to the broken staircase and say:

:   *"The stairs are knocked out. I have no doubt you can find a way up. You never know, you may find something of value up there. I shall look around. We can proceed when you are ready."*

If you make it up to the platform she was referring to, she'll exclaim:

:   *"Impressive! Was it worth the effort?"*

As she reaches the hall full of traps, she'll laugh and say:

:   *"I am not going down there. It would be foolish to attempt it. You have a much better chance than I to make it through these traps. I have no doubt that lever turns these blades off. I shall wait here for now."*

Once you pull the lever, she'll run down the hall and say:

:   *"Thank you. Miraak took great pains to make it difficult to reach him, it seems. Let us hope that is the last of these traps."*

#### Temple of Miraak Sanctum

*"I do not like this place."*

*"This book... It seems wrong, somehow."*

As you enter the Sanctum, Frea will comment:

:   *"I do not know what it is Miraak learned that gave him reason to turn on his masters. But his path seems to have been a cruel one. I wonder if we will find some answers to what happened so long ago."*

Once you reach the next chamber, she'll notice a side passage and say:

:   *"Interesting. This may be worth exploring."*

She'll then follow the passage to a room with treasure and say:

:   *"I suspected there would be something down here. Do you know those spells already?"*

When you press on further, she'll say:

:   *"How much deeper can this be? I had been told that Miraak's power was great, but to have built so large a temple... It cannot be much farther now. I feel it in my bones."*

Once you reach the room with the word wall, she'll say:

:   *"I had heard Miraak had turned against the Dragon Cult, but to display the remains in such a manner as this... It is no wonder the dragons razed his temple to the ground. Seeing the remains hung up like trophies must have enraged them to no end."*

She'll then say:

:   *"Something feels wrong. Brace yourself!"*

After you defeat the [Gatekeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Gatekeeper "Skyrim:Gatekeeper") and travel to the dining area, she'll say:

:   *"Dead end? Impossible. There must be something more! Look around. I will let you know if I find anything in the dining area."*

Once you uncover the secret passage, she'll exclaim:

:   *"I knew it! A secret passage in the dining area just opened up. This must be it. Let us move quickly."*

When you travel to the next chamber, she'll comment:

:   *"I wonder if there is something here that tells the story of Miraak..."*

She'll then say:

:   *"Nothing but ruined books."*

As she heads to the next chamber, she'll run up to the statue and say:

:   *"I do not recognize this statuary. We passed by a few of them earlier, but they are becoming more frequent as we get further in. I do not like this place. It almost looks as if these statues will come to life at any moment."*

She'll pause and then say:

:   *"It looks like there is only one way to proceed. I leave the honor of pulling that handle to you. I do not want to put my hand anywhere near the mouth of that statue."*

As you proceed, she'll say:

:   *"It is eerily quiet. I do not suspect that will be the case the further we go. Be on your guard."*

As you near the black book, she say:

:   *"There are dark magics at work here. Ready yourself. This book... It seems wrong, somehow. Here, yet... not. It may be what we seek."*

After you read the Black Book, Frea will walk up to you and say:

:   *"What happened to you? You read the book and then... It seemed as though you were not really here. I could see you, but also see through you!"*
:   **I'm not really sure. I saw Miraak on a dragon.**
:   *"Where? Where is he? Can we reach him? Can we kill him?"*
:   **Somehow, reading this book took me to where he was.**
:   *"This is a dangerous thing, then. We should return to my village, and show this to my father. Perhaps Storn can make sense of what is going on."*

The next quest, [The Fate of the Skaal](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fate_of_the_Skaal "Skyrim:The Fate of the Skaal"), will then start.

### The Fate of The Skaal

Frea will then exit conversation and say:

:   *"Come, there looks to be a way out through here."*

She'll then run out of the temple and direct you attention to the Wind Stone:

:   *"You see that green light? That comes from the Wind Stone, where my people work against their will. They must be freed soon."*

She'll then say:

:   *"The village is just ahead. Storn has used his magic to raise a barrier around it, protecting the few of us left. That the barrier is still there is a good sign."*

As she dashes towards Storn, she'll tell him the discovery you made in the temple:

*"Frea! What news do you bring?"*

**Frea**: *"Father! I have returned! There is yet hope! "*
**Storn**: *"Frea! What news do you bring? Is there a way to free our people?"* **or**, if Storn sent you to assist Frea, *"Frea! I had worried I would not see you again."*
**Frea**: *"No, but I have brought someone who has seen things... He/She has confirmed that Miraak is indeed behind the suffering of our people."*
**Storn**: *"I feared that it would be so."*
**Frea**: *"But how is that possible? After all this time..."*
**Storn**: *"I fear there is too much we do not yet know."*
**Frea**: (to you) *"Please, tell Storn what has happened."*

Frea will then sit by Storn to assist him with the barrier. When you free the villagers, she will start a new daily routine in the Skaal Village. She now wakes up at 8am and starts her day hanging out in the Shaman's hut for two hours. At 10am, she'll head outside to sit next to Storn on the bench next to their house for three hour and then she will go back into the Shaman's hut and stay there until her bedtime at 10pm.

After you free the Skaal from Miraak, she may now greet you with:

:   *"It's good that our people are now free. We can attempt to restore balance to our home."*

### The Path of Knowledge

Although Frea is not directly involved in this quest, she does have some comments if you have her as follower during the quest. When you initially approach [Nchardak](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchardak "Skyrim:Nchardak"), she'll warn you:

:   *"The Skaal have always avoided ruins such as these. Nothing of the All-Maker is to be found within."*

Once she approaches the Black Book inside the reading room, she'll comment:

:   *"The dwarves must have feared this book to lock it away like this."*

As she enters the Great Chamber, she'll muse:

:   *"Amazing to think that they built this so long ago, and it still survives."*

When you see the fire trap in the Workshop, she'll say:

:   *"It would be madness to go through there."*

As you continue through the workshop, she'll comment:

:   *"It is rather impressive."*

When you approach the southern section of the Workshop, she'll warn you:

:   *"Be careful."*

When you collect the fourth cube, she will converse with [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth"):

:   **Frea**: *"So, we only need one more of these... cubes?"*
:   **Neloth**: *"That's correct. I'm glad to see someone else has been paying attention."*

When you enter the Aqueduct, Neloth will complain about the swimming, to which Frea will respond with:

:   *"You should leave slogging around in the muck to us youngsters."*

When you lower all three bridges in the first chamber, Frea will congratulate you with:

:   *"I think you did it."*

When Neloth tells you to retrieve the last cube without his help, she'll be relieved:

:   *"Finally. We will not have to listen to his complaining."*

When Neloth warns you of the rising water levels, Frea will sarcastically say:

:   *"Thanks for the warning."*

Once you acquire the fifth cube, Frea will muse:

:   *"Now we will see if he knows what he is talking about."*

When you activate the boilers, she'll detect the Centurion:

:   *"Beware! Another of those creatures!"*

If you drop a cube, she'll say:

:   *"Bring that cube. We'll need it."*

### The Gardener of Men

If you had Frea as an active follower during the previous quest, she will then leave your service after you read the Black Book *[Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)")*. If you tell her you need to learn the "secrets of the skaal" to defeat Miraak, she'll direct you to her father:

:   **I need the "secrets of the Skaal" in order to defeat Miraak.**
:   *"You must talk to Storn, then. As shaman, he is the keeper of such lore. I have learned some of what he knows, but it is not my place to divulge anything to an outsider."*

You'll now have two options:

:   **Aren't you his apprentice? He must have taught you his secrets...**
:   *"You will not convince me to betray Storn's trust. Talk to him. He will decide the matter."*

:   **I understand. I'll talk to Storn.**
:   *"Good. Although I do not think he will help you. These secrets are sacred to us."*

If you greet her after asking for the secrets, she'll tell you:

:   *"Only Storn can reveal the secrets you asked about."*

If you ask her to follow you, she'll dismiss you:

:   *"I am sorry, but my duty is to my people right now."*

Once Storn agrees to give up his secrets, she'll try to stop him:

**Frea**: *"Father, you must not do this. That book is... wrong. Evil. Against everything that you have taught me my whole life."*
**Storn**: *"I must, Frea. It is the only way to free Solstheim forever from Miraak's shadow. There comes a time when everything must change. Nothing that lives remains the same forever. Do not fear for me, my daughter. This is the destiny that the All-Maker has laid out for me."*
**Frea**: *"I stand beside you, father, as always."*
**Storn**: *"I am ready for whatever the foul master of this book has in store for me."*

*"I just wish he had seen another way."*

When Hermaeus Mora takes control of Storn, Frea will yell to you:

:   *"What's happening? You must stop it!"*

She'll then yell:

:   *"Father! No, stop!"*

She'll then once again turn to you and shout:

:   *"Do something!"*

After Storn dies, she'll exclaim:

:   *"Father! What have you done!"*

She will then look directly at you:

:   *"Go. My father sacrificed himself so that you could destroy Miraak and lift his master's shadow from the land. Go, then. Kill Miraak. Do not fail."*

She will now only say:

:   *"I think he knew what would happen. He saw his death in that book."*
:   *"Do not let his death be for nothing. Go and stop Miraak."*
:   *"I do not blame you. I know he chose this. I just wish he had seen another way."*
:   *"Leave me to mourn my father. I have no more words for you now."*

### Aftermath

Once [Miraak is defeated](/wiki/Skyrim:At_the_Summit_of_Apocrypha "Skyrim:At the Summit of Apocrypha"), Frea will walk up to you and ask:

:   *"I can feel it. The Tree Stone is free again. The Oneness of the land is restored. Does that mean... is it over? Is Miraak defeated?"*

:   :   **It's over. Miraak is dead.**
    :   *"Then my father's sacrifice... it was not in vain. He died to free us. Tell me... was it the only way? Did he need to die?"*

:   :   **Storn didn't die for nothing. Miraak will never threaten Solstheim again.**
    :   *"Thank you. Whatever your other reasons for acting, you have done the Skaal a great service. We will not forget what you've done."*

:   :   **I killed Miraak. But Hermaeus Mora is still out there.**
    :   *"It was Miraak who threatened Solstheim. With him gone, Herma-Mora has been foiled once again. Tell me, though... my father's death... was it necessary? Was there no other way to destroy Miraak?"*

If you chose the first or last option you'll have three more options:

:   **I couldn't have defeated Miraak without Storn's help.**
:   *"Then... it was the All-Maker's will, as he said. I know I should not doubt it. But it is good to hear, all the same. Thank you."*

:   **Hermaeus Mora killed Storn, remember. Not Miraak.**
:   *"I know. The Skaal will not forget this. Storn's death will become another of the many tales of Herma-Mora's treachery."*

:   **Hermaeus Mora wouldn't have helped me without Storn's sacrifice.**
:   *"Yes, his "help" which did not require him to kill my father. Such is the way of Herma-Mora, the eternal enemy of the Skaal."*

Either way, she'll say:

:   *"One more thing, Skaal-friend, if you will. I know it is not my place, but... may I offer a word of advice... of warning?"*

:   :   **Sure, what is it?**
    :   *"As shaman of the Skaal, I am charged with the spiritual well-being of my people. While you are not of the Skaal, you are Skaal-friend, and so I give you this warning. Herma-Mora forced you to serve him in order to defeat Miraak. Do not let him lure you further down that path. The All-Maker made you Dragonborn for a higher purpose. Do not forget that. Walk with the All-Maker, Skaal-friend."*

:   :   **I don't need your advice.**
    :   *"I understand. Walk with the All-Maker, Dragonborn."*

If you didn't take [Epistolary Acumen](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Epistolary_Acumen_(book) "Skyrim:Black Book: Epistolary Acumen (book)") from [Storn Crag-Strider](/wiki/Skyrim:Storn_Crag-Strider "Skyrim:Storn Crag-Strider")'s body before entering Apocrypha, talk to Frea again and she will give it to you and says *"Here is the foul book that killed Storn. Take it away from here. Throw it into the sea. It is evil."*

When you greet her, she will now mention the loss of her father and her new occupation:

:   *"My father was a noble man, and a true Skaal."*
:   *"My heart is still heavy with the loss of my father."*
:   *"I still cannot believe that Storn is gone."*
:   *"It's an honor to serve the Skaal as shaman, but I still miss my father."*

You can then ask her some questions:

:   **Are you sure you're ready to be Shaman of the Skaal?**
:   *"I have been preparing for it all my life. There is no question that I'm ready, but..."*
:   **But what? What is it?**
:   *"It is not right that I should say this, because I must honor my father's wishes, but this is a path I never chose. I always thought that I would be a great hunter, or even the village chieftain."*
:   **That could still happen, couldn't it?**
:   *"Hah! Not if Fanari has anything to say about it. When it comes to being chieftain, she is like a wolf with her jaws clamped tight upon a fresh kill. But that's alright. The Skaal need a shaman and I know that is my place."*

## Dialogue

If you talk to her in Skaal Village before killing Miraak, she'll talk about the leaders of the Skaal and her possible aspirations in her village:

:   *"For many years now I have attended to Storn, learning his ways."*
:   *"[Fanari](/wiki/Skyrim:Fanari_Strong-Voice "Skyrim:Fanari Strong-Voice") shows what it means to be a leader to the Skaal. In time, perhaps I could lead as well."*
:   *"I have much to learn yet from Storn, if I am to one day become the shaman."*

If you ask where her mother is, she'll say:

:   **Where is your mother?**
:   *"She died when I was very young. She was caught in a terrible snowstorm while returning home from gathering firewood. You must understand that, for the Skaal, life is a constant hardship. We take nothing for granted. We cannot afford to. Between the wolves, the weather and the threats in the south, even a simple task like gathering wood for the fire can turn deadly in an instant."*

    :   **Then why stay here? Why not live somewhere safer?**
    :   *"We are bound to this land, like a great pine with roots that run as deep as the tree is tall. I know it must seem strange to you, but for us, the thought of leaving our village is equally strange. The land and the Skaal are one. There is no other way to say it."*

:   :   **Sooner or later, death comes for us all.**
    :   *"We Skaal do not fear death. We know we will return to the All-Maker and be born anew. Life never truly ends. Death is just a passage from one form to the next."*

If you bring up her fighting abilities and ask her who taught her what she knows, she'll bring up her old mentor:

:   **For a shaman, you fight pretty well. Who trained you?**
:   *"It was Skaf the Giant, our former chieftan*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*, who taught me the ways of battle. He was a great bear of a man, and a fearsome warrior. I used to be terrified of him when I was a little girl. I was a restless and angry child, and Skaf taught me swordplay so that I could, as he used to say, "put that fire to good use." He was a great man and a good leader. I miss him dearly."*

When exiting conversation, she'll simply say:

:   *"Farewell, outsider."*
:   *"All-Maker guide you."*

## Combat Dialogue

| Condition | Dialogue | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Detecting an enemy | *"What was...?"* | *"Is someone there?"* |
| Spotting an enemy | *"I knew I heard something!"* | *"Now we end this!"* |
| *"Look out!"* | *"By the All-Maker!"* |
| *"I will strike like a hawk!"* | |
| When attacked by the player | *"This was a foolish mistake, outsider."* | *"Back to where you came from!"* |
| *"You have left me no choice."* | *"I was a fool to trust you!"* |
| *"You should have known better."* | *"That was foolish of you."* |
| Taunting an enemy | *"Spineless coward!"* | *"You are without courage!"* |
| *"Die!"* | *"I will not fall!"* |
| Attacking a [Cultist](/wiki/Skyrim:Cultist "Skyrim:Cultist") | *"Your master cannot help you now!"* | |
| Attacking a [Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") | *"You've no right to be here, monster!"* | *"Back to where you came from!"* |
| Losing sight of an enemy | *"Come back and fight me!"* | *"Where'd you go?"* |
| Searching for an enemy | *"How long do you think you can hide?"* | *"There is no honor in this."* |
| *"I'll find you eventually."* | *"Going to hide, are you?"* |
| *"Show yourself!"* | |
| Giving up the search | *"No need to be worried, I suppose."* | |
| Reacquiring an enemy | *"There you are!"* | *"Knew I'd find you!"* |
| *"Now we finish this!"* | |
| Defeating an enemy | *"There was no other way it could end."* | *"And so it ends."* |
| *"Victorious again."* | *"I am sorry, but you left me with no choice."* |
| When low on health | *"No more!"* | *"Please, stop!"* |
| Witnesses a crime | *"Why would you do such a thing?"* | *"I doubt that was truly necessary."* |
| Witnesses a murder | *"What... what are you doing?!"* | *"Oh no! No!"* |

## Follower Dialogue

After completing The Fate of the Skaal, you can tell Frea you fight well with her and she should join you: *"Join you? You mean leave the village to journey with you and fight at your side? I'm flattered, but the village is my home. It's very rare for one of the Skaal to leave, and I have responsibilities here."* You will now have a few options:

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| You can trust me. I saved your life, remember? **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"You're right. I suppose the others can get by without me for awhile. Very well, if you need my help, seek me out here in the village."*  **Failed**: *"I am sorry, but I must refuse. I am grateful for your help, but my place is here, with my people. We Skaal are not like you. We do not seek adventure, we wish only to live in peace and to honor our traditions. I hope you understand."* | | | | **Passed**: Frea becomes a [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") **Failed**: Nothing |
| I'll make it worth your while. **(Bribe)** | **Failed**: *"The land provides all that I need. I have no use for your coins."* **or** *"As I've already told you, I have no need of money."* | | | | **Failed**: Nothing |

As a follower, she will say the following greetings:

- *"My thoughts are always with my people."*
- *"Even now, the All-Maker watches over us."*
- *"Where shall we journey next?"*
- *"No matter where the road takes us, my thoughts are of home."*
- *"Is it good to see more of the world, for wisdom is the child of experience."*
- *"Your fearlessness never ceases to impress me."*
- *"You face danger without hesitation."*
- *"Remember what happened to Storn." -While Reading a Black Book*

| Your Line | Frea's Response |
| --- | --- |
| **Follow me, I need your help.** | *"I will follow you, Skaal-friend, but I must return to the village afterward."* **or** *"You have a companion already. You don't need my help."* |
| **Follow me.** | *"I will shadow your steps."* |
| **Wait here.** | *"If that is what you wish."* |
| **I need you to do something.** | *"What would you ask of me?"* |
| **I need to trade some things with you.** | *"Very well."* |
| **It's time for us to part ways.** | If Storn is still alive: *"I need to get back to the village. My father will have need of me."*, else: *"It has been an honor, Skaal-friend."* |

Frea's [Skaal Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Amulet "Skyrim:Skaal Amulet")

## Notes

- Since Frea's amulet is part of her default outfit, it is somewhat more difficult to get her to equip necklaces as a follower, since they typically do not have an armor rating which would outclass her default amulet.
- Although her default gear is governed by the Heavy Armor skill, Frea is actually more proficient in light armor.
  - This issue has been addressed by version 1.0.2 of the [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"); it changes her class to favor heavy armor, and adjusts her perks to match.
- If you visit the Temple of Miraak before starting [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_(quest) "Skyrim:Dragonborn (quest)"), Frea will not be there.
- She is one of the few characters that automatically dual wields, the other being [Rayya](/wiki/Skyrim:Rayya "Skyrim:Rayya"). Even if her war axes are taken away, she will replace them with any other weapons without the need to give her a Forsworn weapon or pickaxe as is the case with most other followers.
- Frea is a very strong follower thanks to her dual wield perks and no level cap.
  - She is also the only follower that both doesn't have a level cap and is essential, meaning there will essentially never be a need to replace her.

## Bugs

- If Frea is your follower during The Path of Knowledge or The Gardener of Men, there's a period where she'll leave you but still take up your follower spot. To avoid this, either dismiss her before reading the Black Book: Epistolary Acumen or right after you return from [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha"), go to the Skaal Village (where she runs to) and dismiss her before speaking with Storn. Otherwise you'll be without a follower until you complete the Dragonborn [main questline](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn_Quests#Main_Quest "Skyrim:Dragonborn Quests"). **?**
- Two of Frea's combat taunts, "This is a foolish mistake, outsider." and "You have left me no choice." are supposed to be directed you, however she can say these lines when she's in combat with anyone else.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.2, addresses this issue. A condition check has been added to each Topic Info, checking that the target is the player, which both Topic Infos currently lack.

# Skyrim:Freir

## Overview

| Freir (RefID: 000198A6) | | | |

Freir

**Freir** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [priestess](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") at the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"). Her husband is [Rorlund](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorlund "Skyrim:Rorlund"), the high priest of the Eight Divines. If you visit the Temple, she will extend an invitation to pray at the shrines and seek the [blessing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessings "Skyrim:Blessings") of the Divines. If questioned about the empty alcove in the Temple, she will explain that it used to have a Shrine of Talos until the worship of [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos") was banned by the [White-Gold Concordat](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat"). If the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take over Solitude, she will change her dialogue to say "Nine Divines" instead of "Eight Divines".

She wakes at 6am and starts working as the temple minister, tending the [shrines](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines "Skyrim:Shrines") for twelve hours. At 6pm, she finishes working and wanders around the place until 12am, when she heads to bed.

Freir wears a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") along with a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When you are near her, she can be found saying things like:

:   *"Blessings of the Eight Divines upon you. How may I help?"* (If the city is under Imperial control)
:   *"Blessings of the Nine Divines upon you. How may I help?"* (If the city is under Stormcloak control)
:   *"You look troubled. Have you come seeking guidance?"*
:   *"Feel free to take a seat, or pray at the shrines. We appreciate worship in all its forms."*

Upon ending a conversation with her, she may tell you:

:   *"The strong and honorable always carry the blessing of the Eight."* (If the city is under Imperial control)
:   *"The strong and honorable always carry the blessing of the Nine."* (If the city is under Stormcloak control)
:   *"Your rewards in life will match the strength of your faith."*

While she is working as minister in the temple, she will pray with:

:   *"May knowledge of your Divinity carry us through our daily trials."*
:   *"Remind us of our place, when we forget."*
:   *"Let us walk in the steps of the Divines."*

She shares this dialogue with [Greta](/wiki/Skyrim:Greta "Skyrim:Greta"), [Silana Petreia](/wiki/Skyrim:Silana_Petreia "Skyrim:Silana Petreia"), and Rorlund.

:   **What do the shrines do?**
:   *"Those who worship at the shrines will sometimes receive boons from the gods themselves. The nature of the favors varies per deity. Please, feel free to worship at any or all of the shrines."*

If Solitude is under control of the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), you can mention to Freir that one of the alcoves up front is empty:

:   **One of the alcoves up front is empty.**
:   *"Hmm? Ah, yes. That once held the shrine to Talos. But the worship of Talos was banned by the White-Gold Concordat, some time ago."*

:   **What's the White-Gold Concordat?**
:   *"It's the peace treaty that ended the war with the Elves of the [Aldmeri Dominion](/wiki/Lore:Aldmeri_Dominion "Lore:Aldmeri Dominion"). The Dominion recognized the heresy of proclaiming Talos a god. Talos was a great man, and a great Emperor... but that does not make him a god. No matter how much the Stormcloaks may wish it were so."*

## Conversations

She and Silana may sometimes talk with each other about the poor in Solitude:

:   **Silana**: *"Mistress, a word?"*
:   **Freir**: *"Certainly, acolyte. What troubles you?"*
:   **Silana**: *"I know you and father Rorlund have many duties to attend to in the temple, but sometimes I feel that there are more important matters to attend to."*
:   **Freir**: *"What could be more important than hearing the prayers of the faithful, and answering the questions of the dedicated?"*
:   **Silana**: *"Mistress, the people of Solitude are destitute. Many are starving and desperate for work. We need to be more active, to reach out to them."*
:   **Freir**: *"We took you in, didn't we? We would be glad to extend our welcome to any other who showed your dedication. What more could we do?"*
:   **Silana**: *"I know, and I appreciate it dearly. But I can't help but feel we could be doing more..."*
:   **Freir**: *"[Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth") has blessed you with tremendous compassion, Silana. You will find a way, I'm sure of it."*

She can also be seen conversing with Rorlund about attendance:

:   **Rorlund**: *"A word, my love?"*
:   **Freir**: *"What troubles you, darling?"*
:   **Rorlund**: *"I fear attendance is down. There are so few worshippers coming to see us. Could it be that the war has weakened their faith?"*
:   **Freir**: *"Nonsense, dear. I've had more visitors than ever seeking the wisdom of the hearth goddesses."*
:   **Rorlund**: *"Ah, that must be it. So many of the men are serving in battle. I shall pray to [Stendarr](/wiki/Lore:Stendarr "Lore:Stendarr") that they return victorious."*

## Notes

- Freir does not have a unique facial model, she instead uses the default female Nord face. She shares this quirk with another woman living at the [Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables"), [Fridrika](/wiki/Skyrim:Fridrika "Skyrim:Fridrika").

## Bugs

- Freir may still discuss the rightness of the White-Gold Concordat and the missing Talos shrine if the Stormcloaks capture Solitude, even though she swaps over to saying "Nine Divines" instead of "Eight Divines" in all her other dialogues if they do.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.4, fixes this bug.

Frida

**Frida** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:VendorApothecary "Skyrim:VendorApothecary") who runs [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). Years ago, her husband died while searching for the [Ring of Pure Mixtures](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Pure_Mixtures "Skyrim:Ring of Pure Mixtures") and she will [ask you](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)") to finish what he started.

She sleeps above the main trading room every night between midnight and 8am. She then heads downstairs where she unlocks the front door and positions herself behind the counter, offering her services for twelve hours. At 8pm she leaves the store and heads up the hill for a four-hour visit to [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") before bedtime.

She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and carries the [shop key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:Key to The Mortar and Pestle") and some [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She wears a regular set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothes") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0004223d "Skyrim:Boots") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#0004223b "Skyrim:Hat").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Further Study](/wiki/Skyrim:Further_Study "Skyrim:Further Study")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Collect a fish to help an alchemist experiment with potions. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

If approached in her shop she can say:

:   *"The Mortar and Pestle makes potions, if you can't tell from the name. Just step up to the counter."*

:   *"A Stamina Potion maybe? Popular with young men."*

:   *"The Mortar and Pestle has cures for every illness, from Ataxia to Witbane."*

:   *"Let me know if you come down with the Rattles."*

:   *"No. I don't have anything for bad dreams, so don't ask."* **(Before [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") is complete)**

:   *"Silus keeps filling his house with those Mythic Dawn things. Creepy, I tell you."*

If you meet her outside her shop, she will instead say:

:   *"Frost took my husband years ago. He was a good man."*

:   *"My children all grew up and left Dawnstar to make their fortune."*

When spoken to directly she can be asked questions:

:   **Have you been in Dawnstar long?**
:   *"Pfft. I'm the oldest woman in Dawnstar. Was here when the [Skald the Elder](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald") was Skald the Younger. He's a fool, if you haven't met him already. Thinks [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") is invincible and spits dragon fire. The people here look to [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") when they need things settled. Real firebrand going*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *up. Wasn't surprised when she joined the Legion."*

If Brina is appointed [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Dawnstar, she will express her support, saying:

:   *"Seems Brina Merilis and the [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") came and now she's Jarl. That's a relief. I don't like the fighting, but Brina is the woman for the job."*

If you choose to invest in her business:

:   **I'd like to make an investment in your business.**
:   *"How kind. At my age, I've certainly learned how to spend wisely."*
:   **Let's see what you can do with this.**
:   *"More coin means more supplies, and that means more useful balms, potions and remedies for everyone."*

### Dungeon Delving (Caves)

When asked about how she picked up the herb trade, she will tell you about her deceased husband and give you a task:

:   **How'd you pick up the herb trade?**
:   *"My husband. We used to go out in the wilds and collect ingredients together. He used to call me his 'pretty Juniper.' It's quite romantic, if you're an alchemist. Frost took the old fool a few seasons back, while he was looking for the Ring of Pure Mixtures. I found the ring's resting place after he died, but I'm far too old to go exploring some cave, now."*

:   **I can't do that right now.**

    :   *"Why am I not surprised?"*

:   **I could find that ring for you.**

    :   *"Well, aren't you sweet? I'd be happy to give you some alchemy training in exchange for the ring, if you bring it to me."*

She will end the conversation with:

:   *"If you find that ring, bring it here."*

When you return with the ring, she will be grateful and provide some free [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") training:

:   **I have your ring.**
:   *"Thank you. Here, let an old alchemist pass on some of her secrets to you."*

## Conversations

When Frida spends time at the Windpeak Inn, she can often be seen talking to either barkeep [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring") or local bard [Karita](/wiki/Skyrim:Karita_(bard) "Skyrim:Karita (bard)").

:   **Frida**: *"Now, who was it that kidnapped the Jarl's son 20 years ago?"*
:   **Thoring**: *"You mean Hildolf the Skull-Splitter? Remember when we rounded up the townspeople and dragged him out of that cave?"*
:   **Frida**: *"Those were the days. I'd never seen my husband fight so bravely before."*
:   **Thoring**: *"Aye, to your husband. Divines bless his memory."*

:   **Frida**: *"Thoring, do you remember the time when that wolf pack come clamoring into town?"*
:   **Thoring**: *"How could I forget? That old alpha male almost took off my leg."*
:   **Frida**: *"Never did find out why they came sprawling into town like that."*
:   **Thoring**: *"Animals in the Pale don't need a reason to attack Dawnstar. It's just their nature."*
:   **Frida**: *"Dawnstar has always held its own against the bandits and wild animals of the Pale."*

:   **Karita**: *"Did you ever have to fight off bandits, Frida? Like in your stories?"*
:   **Frida**: *"Why, I once fought alongside your father when we were both younger. Saved him from getting his fool head sliced off."*
:   **Karita**: *"Who were you fighting against?"*
:   **Frida**: *"Oh, dearie, it was so long ago. But I do remember the celebration we had afterwards. Mead never tasted so good."*

:   **Frida**: *"Did I ever tell you about the day when Skald the Elder was Skald the Younger?"*
:   **Karita**: *"I can't imagine Skald ever being young."*
:   **Frida**: *"Oh, he was young, and handsome. I had half a mind to go after him, myself, before I met my husband."*
:   **Karita**: *"Frida, you aren't saying...."*
:   **Frida**: *"I was a beauty in my day, dearie. Don't act so surprised."*

## Notes

- The guards in Dawnstar might mention her in passing, saying: *"Old lady Frida is a grouch, but she sure can whip up a cure for the Rattles fast."*
- If you have the Merchant perk from the Speech skill line, you will be able to buy the Ring of Pure Mixtures from her, assuming you completed that quest beforehand.

Fridrika

**Fridrika** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Classes#Citizen "Skyrim:Classes") who lives at [Solitude Stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Stables "Skyrim:Solitude Stables") with her husband [Geimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Geimund "Skyrim:Geimund") and son [Horm](/wiki/Skyrim:Horm "Skyrim:Horm"). Geimund owns the Solitude Stables and is a retired mercenary. If he dies Horm will sell the horses.

With her husband in charge of selling the horses, Fridrika helps out with maintaining the small farm behind the stables, although most of her time is spent wandering and looking for potential customers. She sleeps in the stable building every night between midnight and 8am and always starts the day with a one-hour breakfast. At 9am she heads outside and for 11 hours, interrupted only by another one-hour meal at 6pm. At 8pm she heads back inside and wanders around until her bedtime at midnight.

She wears a typical merchant outfit which consists of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223d "Skyrim:Clothing"), [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothing") and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223b "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries a spare [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and a selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Dialogue

When greeting you, Fridrika seems pretty uninterested:

:   *"Is this about the stables? My husband, Geimund, handles the business."* (If Geimund is alive)
:   *"Is this about the stables? With my husband gone, my son Horm handles the business."* (If Geimund is dead)
:   *"A man like you should own a horse. Go speak with my husband."* (If you are male)
:   *"A woman like you should own a horse. Go speak with my husband."* (If you are female)
:   *"I really don't mean to be rude, but I don't think there's much I can help you with."*
:   *"My family's weathered its share of problems, but we don't dwell on the past."*
:   *"Plenty of chores to do..."*

## Notes

- For some reason, Fridrika is marked as a Friend of [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke") in the Creation Kit. This relationship is never explained.
- Fridrika does not have a unique facial model, she instead uses the default female Nord face. She shares this quirk with another Solitude resident, [Freir](/wiki/Skyrim:Freir "Skyrim:Freir").

# Skyrim:Frightened Woman

## Overview

| Frightened Woman | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000B1CFF |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

A frightened woman wandering the wilderness

The **Frightened Woman** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") who appears [randomly](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Mistwatch_Escapee "Skyrim:World Interactions") and provides directions and an updated map marker to [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch").

She wears a typical prisoner's outfit, including a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") and [footwraps](/wiki/Skyrim:Footwraps "Skyrim:Footwraps"). She has a small chance of carrying a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

When you meet her she will seek you out and say:

:   *"Oh, thank goodness! I've been wandering alone for so long, I thought I'd never see another soul again."*
:   **Calm down. Tell me what happened.**
:   *"I was kidnapped by these bandits weeks ago. They locked me up in the towers near Mistwatch. I managed to pick the lock and slip out while the guard slept, but now I'm completely lost. Can you help me, please?"*
:   **There's a town nearby in that direction. Do you need help getting there?**
:   *"Oh, thank you, but I should be fine now that you've shown me the way. But those bandits have to be stopped! They're at Mistwatch. Here, let me show you on your map.... If you can stop them, you'll be a true hero!"*

She will then finish the conversation and run away.

## Notes

- If she isn't killed on the way to the nearest town, she can sometimes be found working as a laborer later in the game.

## Bugs

- The world encounter "Mistwatch Escapee" never removes her from the game after speaking to you about the bandits at [Mistwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistwatch "Skyrim:Mistwatch").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Frodnar

## Overview

| Frodnar (RefID: 0001348B) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home Town | [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood") | | |
| House | [Hod and Gerdur's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod_and_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Hod and Gerdur's House") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child_(class) "Skyrim:Child (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001348B | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001347E |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 0 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") | | |
| Race Details | [Child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") | | |

| [Adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption")[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") | Yes, if orphaned | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleChild](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleChild "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleChild") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionWhiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun "Skyrim:CrimeFactionWhiterun"); [Riverwood Gerdurs House Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Gerdurs_House_Faction "Skyrim:Riverwood Gerdurs House Faction"); [TownRiverwoodFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiverwoodFaction "Skyrim:TownRiverwoodFaction") | | |

Frodnar on the bench outside of the Sleeping Giant Inn

**Frodnar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). He enjoys playing pranks on people and can sometimes be found talking to his friend [Dorthe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dorthe "Skyrim:Dorthe") about pulling a prank. He is often accompanied by a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") named [Stump](/wiki/Skyrim:Stump "Skyrim:Stump") as well.

Frodnar is the son of [Gerdur](/wiki/Skyrim:Gerdur "Skyrim:Gerdur") and [Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod"), who own the local mill. Like his parents, Frodnar is a supporter of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), and has a great deal of respect for his uncle [Ralof](/wiki/Skyrim:Ralof "Skyrim:Ralof").

Frodnar wears [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"), and is equipped with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). He carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Gerdur's House") to [the family's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod_and_Gerdur%27s_House "Skyrim:Hod and Gerdur's House"), a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Related Quests

- **[Before the Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Before_the_Storm "Skyrim:Before the Storm")**: Inform the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") about the dragon attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen").
- **[Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(game) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)")**: Play a round of Hide and Seek with some [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children") in town. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Tag, you're it!](/wiki/Skyrim:Tag,_you%27re_it! "Skyrim:Tag, you're it!")**: Play a round of Tag with the children of a city. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

He thinks very highly of himself and will sometimes say:

:   *"You're new around here, so I'll go easy on ya, but don't get on my bad side."*
:   *"Get me mad, and I'll prank ya. And not a little. A lot."*
:   *"Ah, everybody around here's so serious."*
:   *"So I like to have a little fun, so what."*
:   *"My friend Dorthe doesn't like my pranking. "You're being mean, Frodnar!" So what if I am?"*
:   *"Mother wants me to work at the mill, but I ain't nobody's slave."*
:   *"You gotta have better things to do than talk to me all day..."*

### Before the Storm

Should you choose to accompany Ralof to Riverwood after [escaping from Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), a scene will occur in which Frodnar eagerly asks about the status of the war and professes his desire to join the Stormcloaks:

**Frodnar**: *"Uncle Ralof! Can I see your axe? How many Imperials have you killed? Do you really know [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")?"*
**Gerdur**: *"Hush, Frodnar. This is no time for your games."*
**Frodnar**: *"Aw, mama, I want to stay and talk with Uncle Ralof!"*
**Ralof**: *"Look at you, almost a grown man! Won't be long before you'll be joining the fight yourself."*
**Gerdur**: *"Go and watch the south road. Come find us if you see any [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") coming."*
**Frodnar**: *"That's right! Don't worry, Uncle Ralof, I won't let those soldiers sneak up on you."*

## Conversations

Frodnar is usually seen together with Dorthe and Stump, and can be heard having a conversation about a prank involving Stump:

**Dorthe**: *"Wait, so... a costume? You're not serious..."*
**Frodnar**: *"Sure I am. We get some furs and tree branches, paint them white, and then tie them to Stump. Instant [Frostbite Spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider")!"*
**Dorthe**: *"Frodnar... nobody is going to believe that your dog is a... Frostbite Spider. And if they do... they'll kill him. That's not much of a prank."*
**Frodnar**: *"Oh yeah, and what would you rather do?"*
**Dorthe**: *"How about... we play tag! You're it!"*
**Frodnar**: *"Hey, no fair! Get her, Stump!"*

Sometimes Frodnar and his father Hod can be seen spending some quality time together. When they have a conversation, Hod will usually ask his son about the recent pranks he did, and also encourages him. Frodnar will pick between three random lines and Hod will do the same:

| Speaker | Conversation |
| --- | --- |
| **Hod** | *"Hey boy, I heard you nailed a Septim into [Lucan](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius")'s doorstep. Damn near drove him crazy. That true?"* |
| *"Tell me, son. Any truth to these stories I been hearing. About you gluing a [cow](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow "Skyrim:Cow")'s udders shut? You really do something like that?"* |
| *"Heard me a rumor, boy. Something about you putting bugs in the stew over at the [Sleeping Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn"). You do this?"* |
| **Frodnar** | *"Sure I did. And I'd do it again."* |
| *"Yeah. So?"* |
| *"Ha ha ha ha! Yeah, I sure did. It was one of my best pranks yet, father."* |
| **Hod** | *"Ha ha ha ha ha ha ha! That's my boy!"* |
| *"Ha! I knew it! Had your name written all over it, that one did!"* |
| *"See, now that's what I'm talking about. Working hard, making your mark on this world. Good job, son."* |
| **Frodnar** | *"He he he he he."* |
| *"You just wait. My new pranks are going to the best ever! You'll see! He he he he."* |
| *"Ha! That ain't nothing. Wait till you see what I got planned for next week."* |

## Notes

- If you escaped Helgen with Ralof, he will be flagged as a parent for Frodnar if Hod and Gerdur are killed.

## Bugs

- Frodnar may be stuck at times, standing idly alone at the center of Riverwood, no matter the time of the day, how long you wait, or how much time you leave Riverwood.
  A possible fix is entering and leaving the house (Alvor's or Hod & Gerdur's) where his dog Stump is. **?**
- If Frodnar is orphaned and you [adopt](/wiki/Skyrim:Adoption "Skyrim:Adoption") him, Stump will continue to follow Frodnar, causing him to travel from Riverwood to your house and back every day.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Frodnar's bed isn't a child's bed, causing him to either sleep in his parents' bed or stay up all night.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, addresses this issue. His bed wasn't marked as a child's bed, making it impossible for him to use it.

# Skyrim:Frofnir Trollsbane

## Overview

| Frofnir Trollsbane (RefID: 0003E8AC) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | Between [Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower") and [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume") [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-105567&y=-31508.2&zoom=17&legacy=true) | | |

Frofnir's body

**Frofnir Trollsbane** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be found deceased in a troll's den between [Cradle Stone Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradle_Stone_Tower "Skyrim:Cradle Stone Tower") and [Valthume](/wiki/Skyrim:Valthume "Skyrim:Valthume"). An easy way of finding him is to find the [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") that is to the west of Cradle Stone Tower and then rock climb north-northwesterly down to him, near two [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll").

He wears a full set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") and carries a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield"), a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") supplemented by [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), and the unique warhammer [Trollsbane](/wiki/Skyrim:Trollsbane "Skyrim:Trollsbane").

## Notes

- There is a dead [elk](/wiki/Skyrim:Elk "Skyrim:Elk") and a portion of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") as well as numerous troll skulls, other human and animal bones scattered around him. Further to the west are several bird's nests with either [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") or [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg").

Froki's Shack

**Froki's Shack** is a small [shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Shacks "Skyrim:Shacks") southeast of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead").

The [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") hunter [Froki Whetted-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki_Whetted-Blade "Skyrim:Froki Whetted-Blade") lives here with his grandson [Haming](/wiki/Skyrim:Haming "Skyrim:Haming"), a survivor of [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). He is a follower of the old ways and a devout worshipper of [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"). Froki will guide you through the [Sacred Trials of Kyne](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials") if you allow him. It consists of one area, *[Froki's Shack](#Froki.27s_Shack)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Froki Whetted-Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki_Whetted-Blade "Skyrim:Froki Whetted-Blade")  [Haming](/wiki/Skyrim:Haming "Skyrim:Haming") |

## Related Quests

- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance is a basket containing a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), two loose [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), and a quiver of the same, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") nearby. To the right of the door is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). In the cliff below the shack, there is an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") with a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond") visible and collectible on the surface of the vein. There is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the ground beside the vein. A [purple mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") grow near the [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block").

A [shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines") can be found outside the shack farther south in the mountains, surrounded by [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"), an [Imperial light shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Light Shield"), a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[King](/wiki/Skyrim:King "Skyrim:King")*, a copy of *[The Amulet of Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Amulet_of_Kings "Skyrim:The Amulet of Kings")*, a satchel, five loose [gold coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [heavy Imperial helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet"), and an [Imperial sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). There are two [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes on the way from the shack to the shrine.

### Froki's Shack

The shack's interior

Upon entering, you will find a [steel battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Steel Battleaxe") to the left of the door. There is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") on your left, with a large shelving unit next to it. The shelves hold a woodcutter's axe, an [eye of sabre cat](/wiki/Skyrim:Eye_of_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Eye of Sabre Cat"), a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") skill book *[Vernaccus and Bourlor](/wiki/Skyrim:Vernaccus_and_Bourlor "Skyrim:Vernaccus and Bourlor")*, a [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot"), and an [orange dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"). A small table and two chairs are opposite the door, with a [luna moth wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing") and a [butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing") on the table. Against the southeast wall is a single bed and an unlocked chest containing minor loot.

## Notes

- Even after you complete the trials and Froki says he counts you "as a friend," the items in the shack can't be taken without stealing.
- Though Haming lives here with his grandfather, there is only one small bed, and Froki sleeps in it.
-  Version 2.1.2 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch") marks the basket, leather strip, iron arrows, and woodcutter's axe just outside the shack as owned.

## Bugs

- On the wood chopping block outside to the north-northwest of the shack, you can find a respawning [Diadem of the Savant](/wiki/Skyrim:Diadem_of_the_Savant "Skyrim:Diadem of the Savant"). It is likely this was a mistake, as the Creation Kit specifies the diadem was meant to be a unique reward for completing [Shalidor's Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Maze "Skyrim:Shalidor's Maze").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.5, addresses this issue. It changes this instance of the diadem into a leveled circlet with a [Fortify Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Apparel#Fortify_Archery "Skyrim:Generic Magic Apparel") effect.
- The woodcutter's axe may be partially embedded into the wood chopping block, making the Diadem of the Savant or the archery circlet hard to pick up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The floor of the shack is higher than it should be. This is evident from the door's position on the inside, the low ceiling, and the proximity of the mounted animal heads to the chairs and table. **?**

Froki Whetted-Blade

**Froki Whetted-Blade** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ranger](/wiki/Skyrim:Ranger_(class) "Skyrim:Ranger (class)") who lives in [his shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Shack "Skyrim:Froki's Shack") alongside his grandson [Haming](/wiki/Skyrim:Haming "Skyrim:Haming"), a survivor of the attack on [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Haming's parents, [Torolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Torolf "Skyrim:Torolf") and [Matlara](/wiki/Skyrim:Matlara "Skyrim:Matlara"), died at Helgen. Froki wears middle class [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000261c0 "Skyrim:Clothing"), [hide bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"), [Kyne's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Token "Skyrim:Kyne's Token"), and a [Ring of Minor Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Minor_Archery "Skyrim:Ring of Minor Archery"). He is equipped with a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and five [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow").

## Related Quests

- **[Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials")**: Participate in [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne")'s Sacred Trials by hunting the guardian beasts of [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim").

### Kyne's Sacred Trials

His greetings:

:   *"Just what we need. City folk barging in, probably looking for an offering to their precious [Divines](/wiki/Lore:Eight_Divines "Lore:Eight Divines")."*
:   *"Well, look at this. Another city rat crawled outside the walls. I don't suppose you've come up here to tell old Froki about your supposed Divines?"*

Speaking to him:

:   **Not me. I don't believe in the Divines.**
:   *"Good. This is Skyrim, and we should honor the old ways. These foreigners don't even respect their own gods, much less Kyne and her Sacred Trials."*

:   **What's wrong with the Divines?**
:   *"They're stolen idols! Imposter gods, sold by silver tongues. No thank you. Froki will not forget [Kyne](/wiki/Lore:Kyne "Lore:Kyne"), or her Sacred Trials."*
:   **Tell me about Kyne.**
:   *"Those sycophants in the Temple would call her Kynareth. Just a pale shadow of the truth, like all the Temple Divines. Kyne! Blessed Warrior-Wife. Shor's widow, sacred to any true Nord hunter. She's the mother of men and beasts, and her veil is the storm."*
:   **What are the Sacred Trials?**
:   *"It's an old Nord Tradition, a test to prove your worth in the eyes of Kyne. Show that you're a hunter and no simple butcher. Kyne teaches us to respect the beasts and blesses the hunter who will face their champions. True Nord hunters are those who survive the Trials. Do you think you're strong enough for Kyne's blessing? I would be glad to pass this tradition down."*

:   :   **I'm not interested.**
    :   *"That's what an old man gets for thinking the younger generation might be interested in learning some honor."*

:   :   **Yes. Tell me what to do.**
    :   *"You must defeat guardian beasts, blessed by Kyne."*

If you accept you can continue with:

:   **What do I need to do?**
:   *"I'll anoint you with the symbol of the wolf, the crab and the skeever. This will compel the guardian to appear when you reach his lair. Return when you've defeated the guardian wolf, crab and skeever."*
:   **A guardian skeever? Are you serious?**
:   *"Don't mock it, pup. Even the lowliest beasts can kill the weak and arrogant. We'll try more powerful enemies next, if you survive this."*

Returning after killing the guardians:

:   **I've defeated the guardians.**
:   *"Maybe you're not so soft, after all. Now you're ready for a real challenge. I'll anoint you with the symbol of the Bear, the Sabrecat and the Mammoth. Tread carefully, these are mighty beasts."*

He can be spoken to further:

:   **What should I do now?**
:   *"The guardian spirits of Bear, Mammoth and Sabre Cat await you. Return when they are defeated."*

After defeating the guardians:

:   **I've defeated the guardian spirits.**
:   *"You do Kyne proud. Only one challenge remains. Go and defeat the troll champion."*

:   **What should I do now?**
:   *"Kyne's guardian troll awaits you. Complete this trial and you'll have proven yourself a true hunter."*

After defeating the guardian troll:

:   **I've defeated the guardian troll.**
:   *"Then you finally know what it means to be a true hunter, in the Nord way. For this you have earned the Blessing of Kyne, and can count me as a friend."*

## Dialogue

If you find [Froki's bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Froki%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Froki's Bow") in [Graywinter Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Graywinter_Watch "Skyrim:Graywinter Watch"), you can mention the bow to him after completing the quest. He'll be surprised to see it:

:   **I found this bow. Is it yours?**
:   *"I don't believe it. I made that bow myself. Been through some messes with it, let me tell you. You know what? I want you to keep it. My great hunts are behind me, but yours are yet to come."*

During Kyne's Sacred Trials, you can ask Froki if Haming is his son. He will correct you, saying, *"Grandson. He's a strong lad. His parents were at Helgen when, well you know."* Further asking him if he likes having Haming around will have him confess, *"Can't say I was a great father the first time around. Now that he's here it's like a second chance. He's a good lad."*

Froki in Sovngarde

## Notes

- If Froki dies, you will meet him again during the quest [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(quest) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (quest)"), sitting on a rock halfway to the Hall of Valor. This version of Froki has a base ID of `000EA57E` and a ref ID of `000EA580`.
- If you obtain [Kyne's Token](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Token "Skyrim:Kyne's Token") from him, either through Kyne's Sacred Trials or by looting it off of his body, and he is also killed before Sovngarde is visited, you can take Kyne's Token from him again in Sovngarde. This allows for two Kyne's Tokens to be obtained.
- Froki has no crime faction assigned and will therefore talk to [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf") and [Vampire Lords](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard").

## Bugs

- Froki may refuse to speak to you after completing his quest even if you have yet to speak to him about his bow.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:From-Deepest-Fathoms

## Overview

| From-Deepest-Fathoms (RefID: 00019DE2, 00056554) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") | | |
| Location | [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"), outside of [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") | | |
| Race | [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") | Gender | Female |
| Level | PC×1 (range=4-7) | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00019DE2 00056554 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001335A 00056553 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50+(PC-1)×8.3 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50+(PC-1)×3.3 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50+(PC-1)×3.3 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy")**, **[Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting")**, **[Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing")**, [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor"), [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak"), [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") | | |
