From-Deepest-Fathoms

Ghostly form

**From-Deepest-Fathoms** is a disturbed [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") who can be found wandering around the docks outside [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery"). She's in possession of a [particular item](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") she would like to see returned to its [place of origin](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel"), due to it carrying too many bad memories for her.

She wears a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), including the [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Helmet "Skyrim:Hide Helmet"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), and the [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") along with a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.
- **[Spread the Love](/wiki/Skyrim:Spread_the_Love "Skyrim:Spread the Love")**: Distribute religious [literature](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") to the citizens of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Dialogue

Once she gets enabled at level 14, Fathoms will be wandering around the dockside, spouting out disturbing warnings to anyone that comes close to her:

:   *"It is done. I won't go back to Avanchnzel. I won't."*
:   *"I could have left it behind. I could have put it back where it came from."*

### Unfathomable Depths

If you speak to the disturbed Argonian wandering around the docks, she will insistently tell you:

:   *"You. You must take the Lexicon. Free me of my burden."*

:   **Lexicon? Burden? What are you talking about?**
:   *"The memories. I cannot stand them. You must take them away, return them to Avanchnzel. You must take the Lexicon from me. Please... take it now."*

:   :   **It's okay. I'll take the Lexicon.**
    :   *"You must bring it to Avanchnzel, in the west. Return it to them. It must go back."*

:   :   **I don't want the Lexicon.**
    :   *"I won't be the one to go back there. I won't return to Avanchnzel. You can't make me do it."*

If you decide to exit dialogue at any point before accepting to return the Lexicon, she will plead:

:   *"Please don't leave. You must help me."*

Once you have accepted, attempting to speak with her further will just result in more cryptic speech:

:   *"Please take the Lexicon."*
:   *"It's yours now. I won't take it back. I won't."*
:   *"Avanchnzel. Take it to Avanchnzel. You must take it back."*

As you first enter Avanchnzel you will see a ghostly vision of the past. It shows a group consisting of Fathoms, as well as three other party members: [Drennen](/wiki/Skyrim:Drennen "Skyrim:Drennen"), [Breya](/wiki/Skyrim:Breya "Skyrim:Breya"), and the apparent leader, [Watches-The-Roots](/wiki/Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots "Skyrim:Watches-The-Roots"):

:   **Drennen**: *"I don't like this place. It feels like we're being... watched."*
:   **Breya**: *"It's a simple job, Drennen. We get in, we steal the Lexicon, we leave. Don't get jumpy."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"If you two cannot handle this, we can find others to hire."*
:   **Roots**: *"Enough. Their services will be more than adequate. Let us continue."*

In the first chamber of the Animoncultory, you will yet again encounter the ghosts, this time trying to break into one of the many hidden chambers of Avanchnzel. At this point, it is clear the place is starting to get to them:

:   **Breya**: *"I told you we should have hired a thief."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"We are thieves, you fool. We're stealing the cube."*
:   **Breya**: *"And yet none of us can pick a damned lock."*

While the apparitions will continue recalling their journey alongside you, Fathoms appears at several points, but doesn't speak. This goes until you reach a campsite in Avanchnzel Animoncultory:

:   **Drennen**: *"This place is huge."*
:   **Roots**: *"It is large, indeed. I did not anticipate Avanchnzel's size or the time needed to uncover the entrance. A few hours sleep and we should be ready to continue through."*
:   **Drennen**: *"Maybe we should turn back. I don't want to sleep here."*
:   **Roots**: *"Drennen, you do understand that the Lexicon at the bottom of this place holds the accumulated memories of centuries of Dwemer."*
:   **Breya**: *"Not to mention our pay."*
:   **Drennen**: *"So?"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"So we're not turning back, you fool."*
:   **Breya**: *"Besides, you're not afraid of a few sleeping metal men. Are you, Drennen?"*

Just before the doors to the Avanchnzel Boilery, Fathoms will give her final thoughts on Drennen:

:   **Drennen**: *"I can't do this. We shouldn't be here. I'm sorry."*
:   **Breya**: *"Drennen!"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Let the field mouse run. Your pay will be double."*
:   **Breya**: *"My pay will be nothing if we die in here!"*
:   **Roots**: *"Calm yourself, Breya. We are closing in on the Lexicon. I can feel it calling. We'll continue without Drennen."*

As you enter the Boilery:

:   **Roots**: *"We are close now. Can you feel the Lexicon calling out?"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Sure."*
:   **Breya**: *"So we get it and get out, right?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Once we have the Lexicon, we'll need to take it to its podium. I know what to do from there. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be mine."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Ours. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be ours."*
:   **Roots**: *"Of course."*

After you have witnessed this scene, the vision Fathoms will no longer appear, but she was meant to make one more appearance, explaining how she ended up in Riften, but this scene can't play due to a [bug](#Bugs). Once the quest is finished, you can return to Fathoms in Riften, but she will make no mention of the events transpired and will not offer you any unique dialogue at all.

### Spread The Love

Despite not appearing to be in the right headspace, you can still offer Fathoms a [religious pamphlet](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warmth_of_Mara "Skyrim:The Warmth of Mara") from the Temple. While she isn't exactly appreciative, she still seems uncharacteristically level-headed:

:   **Here, brother *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*. Blessings of Mara upon you.**
:   *"I have no desire to seek religion."*

## Notes

- From-Deepest-Fathoms will only get enabled once you reach level 14. While her AI immediately makes her move to the docks, she actually gets enabled inside of [Haelga's Bunkhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Haelga%27s_Bunkhouse "Skyrim:Haelga's Bunkhouse"). She also in the faction for the patrons of this establishment, although she can never be found there once she leaves to go wander at the docks.
- Fathoms does not need to be alive in order to start the quest. You only need to receive the Lexicon. This can also be accomplished by pickpocketing it off of her, or looting it off her corpse, or from her coffin in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Riften) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Riften)"), in case her body has been removed. The quest stages will still state you received the Lexicon from her, however.
- From-Deepest-Fathoms has a ghostly form that you encounter while inside Avanchnzel, which uses her second form ID and ref ID and is in the [Dwarven Automaton Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automaton_Faction "Skyrim:Dwarven Automaton Faction").
- Unlike most Argonians with hyphenated names, Fathoms does not use the last part of her name as her "short name" in the subtitles. Instead, her short name is set as "Fathom", which is likely the result of a typo.
- There are 13 different dialogue scenes set up for the quest Unfathomable Depths, but not all of them contain dialogue. The first scene `MS04Vision01Scene`, appears to have been a conversation between Fathoms and Breya, but its contents are unknown.
- Unused scripting in the quest Unfathomable Depths would've given every member of the party a full set of Dwarven armor, although this never happens, and it's unknown what purpose this would've served.

## Bugs

- She is incorrectly referred to as "brother" when handing her a flier during Spread The Love.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- A scene near the giant Dwemer factory may be missing, since the trigger for it is located outside of the map: **?**

:   **Fathoms**: *"The Lexicon had better be worth all this trouble."*
:   **Roots**: *"I assure you, it is. The knowledge contained in the Lexicon created everything you see around you. Properly controlled, it has knowledge enough to turn paupers into kings."*
:   **Drennen**: *"You sure that's power we're meant to have?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Absolutely."*

- Due to a spelling error in the game code, the final scene near the Centurion will never play as intended. It was meant to describe the death of Breya and how Fathoms escaped:

:   **Fathoms**: *"I have the Lexicon! Where's the podium?"*
:   **Breya**: *"I can't hold these things! We need to leave!"*
:   **Fathoms**:*"I did not come all the way here just to walk out empty-handed."*
:   **Breya**:*"The way out is right there! Run, damn it!"*

    -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. However it later became evident that the "fix" actually broke the scene further, and so the changes were reverted by version 2.0.0 of the Unofficial Patch.

# Skyrim:From the Ashes

## Overview

All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project"). | |  |  | | --- | --- | | Prerequisites: | Main Dragonborn quest not running or you've been pointed towards Miraak's temple | | |

Talvas Fathryon has accidentally summoned an ash guardian

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") and go up to the main floor.
2. (Optional) Talk to [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") as you exit Tel Mithryn.
3. Kill the [ash guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian") near the tower.
4. Return to Talvas Fathryon for your reward.

## Detailed Walkthrough

*"It's on your head if something goes wrong."*

When you arrive in Tel Mithryn, you'll find [Talvas Fathryon](/wiki/Skyrim:Talvas_Fathryon "Skyrim:Talvas Fathryon") and [Varona Nelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Varona_Nelas "Skyrim:Varona Nelas") in the middle of an argument. Talvas is attempting to summon an [ash guardian](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Guardian "Skyrim:Ash Guardian"), but is having no luck. Enter the [main tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)") of Tel Mithryn, go up to the main floor, then go back outside. As soon as you leave, you'll see Talvas' summoning has finally worked. He'll run to you in a panic: the ash guardian he got is hostile!

You'll have several reply options. However, even if you tell him to clean up his own mess it's no use: the quest will start and the enemy nearby will disable fast travel. Head down the stipe of the mushroom and confront the ash guardian out in front of Tel Mithryn. Be prepared for a tough fight at lower levels: this creature is level 30 and spews ash at long range that is also wide-arcing.

Once the wayward summon is defeated, you'll have to talk to Talvas again. He's fled into Neloth's tower, so go find him. *"What a relief,"* he says once you have reported in. *"I don't have any gold I can pay you with, but I can give you this staff."* He will then prove true to his word and present you with a [staff](/wiki/Skyrim:Staves "Skyrim:Staves"). In addition, you can now purchase the spell tome for Conjure Ash Guardian from him and recruit him as a follower.

## Notes

- You must go up to the main floor of Tel Mithryn to advance this quest—merely entering and exiting the tower does not work.
- You don't have to speak with Talvas when he's summoned the Ash Guardian. You can, for example, fast travel away and when you come back, you can kill the Ash Guardian without ever speaking with Talvas.
- The Ash Guardian does not leave any remains behind after its death.
- If you traded with Talvas outside, you will have to wait for him to restock his inventory before the Conjure Ash Guardian spell book becomes available.
- If the Ash Guardian hasn't yet been destroyed, you can tell Neloth "Talvas summoned an Ash Guardian outside." Neloth will reply *"What? That fool. His incompetence made this mess. Let's see how he decides to clean it up."*
- If your [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") skill is at least 65, Talvas gives you your choice of a random staff or the spell tome for Conjure Ash Guardian.
- If you have a follower with you when the quest has begun, they may kill the Ash Guardian while you and Talvas are talking to each other. You should be able to talk to him immediately after that to get your reward.

## Quest Stages

| From the Ashes (DLC2TTF1) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | *Objective 100:* Destroy the Ash Guardian |
|  | Talvas has asked me to destroy an Ash Guardian that is running amok on the Tel Mithryn grounds. |
|  | I've encountered an Ash Guardian that is running amok on the Tel Mithryn grounds. |
| 200 |  | *Objective 100:* Destroy the Ash Guardian  *Objective 200:* Talk to Talvas |
| 300 | ☑ | I destroyed the Ash Guardian that Talvas had accidentally summoned. He was quite grateful. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 5, 7, 10, 30, 50, 310, 320, 400.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTF1 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTF1`.

# Skyrim:Frorkmar Banner-Torn

## Overview

| Frorkmar Banner-Torn (RefID: 00077D61, 00037F97) | | | |

| [Essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs") | Yes | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleNordCommander](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNordCommander "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNordCommander") | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CWDialogueSoldierFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:CWDialogueSoldierFaction "Skyrim:CWDialogueSoldierFaction"); [CWFieldCOFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:CWFieldCOFaction "Skyrim:CWFieldCOFaction"); [CWSonsFactionNPC](/wiki/Skyrim:CWSonsFactionNPC "Skyrim:CWSonsFactionNPC"); [CWSonsFieldCOVoiceTypeFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:CWSonsFieldCOVoiceTypeFaction "Skyrim:CWSonsFieldCOVoiceTypeFaction"); [Faction for CW soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Faction_for_CW_soldiers_(excludes_guard_dialogue) "Skyrim:Faction for CW soldiers (excludes guard dialogue)"); [Guard Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Guard_Faction_(for_dialogue) "Skyrim:Guard Faction (for dialogue)"); [Sons of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Sons_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Sons of Skyrim"); [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") | | |

Frorkmar Banner-Torn

**Frorkmar Banner-Torn** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Soldier_(class) "Skyrim:Soldier (class)") and commander of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") who can be found in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). He is usually in [The White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall") or upstairs sleeping in the barracks. If [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is taken by the Imperials, he will relocate to the [Pale Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Pale Stormcloak Camp").

He wears a full set of [Stormcloak officer armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Armor "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Armor"), including matching pairs of [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Bracers "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Bracers") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Boots "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Boots"), and the trademark [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Officer_Helmet "Skyrim:Stormcloak Officer Helmet"). He is equipped with a leveled [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") and a leveled [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and also has a [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons"). He also carries a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") supplemented with 12 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger").

## Dialogue

When you have not joined either the Stormcloaks or the Imperial Legion he can say:

:   **How does one join the Stormcloaks?**
:   *"[Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak")'s not running a social club. You don't join anything. Either you're a true son of Skyrim, or you're not. If you are, then you make your way to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") and talk to the man himself. If you're not, well friend, you'd best walk away before this gets ugly."*

:   **How do you feel about this war?**
:   *"Skyrim is the birthplace of humanity. The birthplace of honor. And those snowbacked Imperials renounced both when they laid down before the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). Worse still, to pay for the privilege to keep his throne, the [Emperor](/wiki/Skyrim:Emperor_Titus_Mede_II_(real) "Skyrim:Emperor Titus Mede II (real)") sells our very gods - [Talos](/wiki/Lore:Talos "Lore:Talos"), no less! - to the damn [elves](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf"). And what did [Torygg](/wiki/Skyrim:High_King_Torygg "Skyrim:High King Torygg") do? He and the [Jarls](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") who supported him? They took the Emperor's gold. Sold out their people for a slave master's "[peace treaty](/wiki/Lore:White-Gold_Concordat "Lore:White-Gold Concordat")." Ulfric did right killing him. Soon we'll rid Skyrim of elves, their bloody Justiciars, and the Jarls in their pockets. The whole damn lot of them. And we'll cleave through the Legion to get to them."*

:   **Why are you called Stormcloaks?**
:   *"At first they called us that to belittle our cause. But we gladly accept being named for Ulfric Stormcloak, the only true High King of Skyrim. We are the true sons and daughters of Skyrim, and Ulfric... he's the truest of us all. We fight to make our land great once more, to raise up strong, noble [thanes](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane"), and lay low false Jarls and the cowards who hide behind them. The sound of our fury is a storm about to break on the heads of our enemies. Our friendship, a cloak of true brotherhood for all who would wear it."*

## Related Quests

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Imperial) "Skyrim:A False Front (Imperial)")**: Find and deliver some forged [documents](/wiki/Skyrim:StormCloak_Documents "Skyrim:StormCloak Documents") to the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

# Skyrim:Frossel

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Frossel ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Frossel)) | | |

| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Frossel

**Frossel** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") on a peninsula north of [Skaal Village](/wiki/Skyrim:Skaal_Village "Skyrim:Skaal Village") containing [bristlebacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback") and [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). It contains only one zone, *[Frossel](#Frossel)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

There are eight [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants producing [ashen grass pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod"), a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant, and three [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") on the shore around the entrance. There is also a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") to the right of the entrance next to a crate. Just south of the entrance are two dead [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") on the shore, among the remains of a camp with a boat, a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"), and a few [riekling spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Spear "Skyrim:Riekling Spear") scattered about.

### Frossel

Frossel begins as an ice tunnel descending to the east. On the left side of the tunnel as you descend is a crate with a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt") and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") on top. Near the bottom is an ice pillar in the middle of the tunnel, with a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") on a crate beside it. When the tunnel turns to the south, look to the corner for a barrel with a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") on top. There are many [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), and other crockery and clutter throughout the cave.

Riekling camp

The tunnel opens into a chamber with four rieklings and two bristlebacks. A small fenced ledge in front of you holds a piece of [refined moonstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Refined_Moonstone "Skyrim:Refined Moonstone") and a deer pelt. The path down is to the left. On the left as you reach the cavern floor are two barrels; one is a fish barrel, and each has a sample of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers") on top. Beneath the ledge via which you entered the chamber, among some riekling tents, crates, sacks, and barrels, there is a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), two [chicken breasts](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Chicken Breast"), a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") (see bugs), three samples of [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), a riekling hut, and two barrels containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients").

To the right of the riekling hut is an unlocked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a drum, an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem"), and a piece of [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") all on what appears to be an archery target laid on a rock, with a piece of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") on the ground in front. The chamber continues to the east. To the left of a bristleback pen is an ice pillar, with two unusable barrels beside it. On these barrels is a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and a plate with a rare [beehive husk](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk") on top. To the right of the pen is another tent with a deer pelt, two iron ingots, a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") (see bugs), and a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek").

A tunnel exits to the east. Along the tunnel are five bottles of wine, including one inside a bucket. On the right just before a corner is another unlocked strongbox on a rock. Farther along are more crates and barrels; among these, you will find a drum, a piece of firewood, three pieces of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot").

Claw trap

A [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") at the bottom of the tunnel triggers a hinged [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap. To the left is an unlocked chest flanked by two [riekling barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Barrel "Skyrim:Riekling Barrel"), which will burst open to reveal two rieklings. A set of small antlers and a [cup](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup") will get scattered when the barrels burst. Behind the chest is a fish barrel, and to the right, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") lies on top of another, empty chest. In the easternmost section of this chamber is a tent, with another riekling ready to ambush you from beneath the snow in front of the tent. Inside the tent, among unusable barrels and crates is a large coin purse and a leveled [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). To the right of the tent, on a crate is a [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore") and a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") in a wooden bowl. To the right on another crate is a random [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"),[†](#intnote_1) and on the ground is an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox").

Opposite the two riekling barrels to the south is an empty chest to the left of a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"). To the right of the vein is a tent with crates and an unusable barrel inside. On the barrel is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") that can be harvested, and on a crate is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). Opposite the tripwire to the south is a riekling hut, with a barrel containing ingredients beside it. The tunnel continues to the west, past an empty chest. After another riekling barrel ambush next to a barrel of meat, the tunnel turns to the south. There are two rieklings in the small, narrow chamber ahead. A large coin purse is on a rock to the right. In a short alcove on the left, there's a riekling barrel in front of an unlocked chest. The unique [Imperial war horn](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_War_Horn "Skyrim:Imperial War Horn") is found here, along with a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and seven loose coins.

Strange sculpture

Worshippers

At the next corner, there is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on the ground (see bugs) and a pair of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") in an open crate. Farther along are two bowls on a crate next to a food barrel; one bowl holds four [small pearls](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"), and the other holds a [Nordic barnacle](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Barnacle "Skyrim:Nordic Barnacle") and a [pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl"). On top of the barrel is a sample of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), as well as two [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg") in another bowl. The tunnel then opens to the main chamber of the cave.

In the main chamber is a curious sight: a group of seven rieklings worshipping a strange idol. A mounted riekling observes from the side. Following the ledge along the eastern wall to the right, you will come upon a riekling hut and a sample of wheat in an adjacent tent. To the left at the entrance is a ramp down to the cavern floor. Any sounds of fighting may draw two more rieklings from a passage beyond. Under the ledge in the northwest section of the chamber is a boss chest near many crates, barrels, and sacks, among which are a total of sixteen loose coins, five silver ingots, two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a [silver garnet ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Garnet_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Garnet Ring"), two [silver rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), four small coin purses, three [silver necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), two [gold necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"), a [corundum ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ingot "Skyrim:Corundum Ingot"), a pair of fine boots, a pair of fine shoes, two sets of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), two fish barrels, a random enchanted [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), a [fine hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Hat "Skyrim:Fine Hat"), a candlestick, two empty, open chests, a [gold ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue"), and four barrels containing ingredients.

To the southeast, past a tent that contains nothing of interest, is an open pen with a mead barrel in the corner against the ledge, with three bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), a woodcutter's axe, a random shield, and a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") lying on the ground near it. To the southwest, between the pen and a gold ore vein and on top of some barrels, there is a broken cart holding five pieces of firewood, a gourd, and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). Northwest of the cart is a ramp leading up to the ledge with the strange idol on top, and to the left of the ramp is another cart containing three pieces of iron ore and a leather strip. To the right of the gold ore vein is a pickaxe on a barrel, and farther to the right is a tent containing clutter. Continuing along the wall to the right, there is a barrel with a gourd and two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg") on top, and farther along another stack of crates with several sacks and more clutter among them.

Treasure

To the left of where the rieklings are worshipping is a flat-topped rock with several crates and barrels around it. There is a deer pelt, an empty soul gem, and a leather strip here, while on top of the rock is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute") in a basket. In the western corner of the main chamber, near the top of the ramp leading up to the strange idol, there is a [steel ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") on a barrel.

An icy tunnel exits the main chamber from the ledge to the north. A short way up the tunnel is a chicken's egg in a wooden bowl on the ground, with a fish barrel and a crate on your left, followed by a gold ore vein on the west wall. The path ascends to a switchback, then up to a second switchback, where a wooden block holds an iron dagger, a bulb of garlic, two samples of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), and a [slaughterfish egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"). On the west wall here is another gold ore vein. Continuing up the path, you will pass some barrels and crates with a [snow fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Snow Fox Pelt") and a cabbage on top, plus three random potions in an open box. The path continues to the top, where there is a bowl containing a leek, with a piece of [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") and a couple cheese wheels beside it. There is an ice tunnel heading to the southeast, with a bowl on the ground containing a red apple, and farther along another goat cheese wheel and a cast iron pot with a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") inside. The tunnel ends at a ledge above the first chamber near the exit. To the left on the ledge before you drop down is a drum and a deer pelt.

## Notes

[†](#note_1)The appearance of this spell tome is complicated. The tome is first randomly selected from all expert-level tomes, then your level in the corresponding skill is checked, and the tome will only appear if your relevant skill is 65 or above. So, unless all your magic skills are at least 65, there is a chance you will not see a tome here.

- Under the ramp leading up to the alcove overlooking the first chamber of the cave is a unique glazed urn which cannot be picked up. However, a jug with a similar appearance can be found in the middle of the chamber.
- An unused safe internally known as `DLC2FrosselSafewithLock` was once intended to appear in this cave. This unique safe would have contained a [fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(item) "Skyrim:Fork (item)"), a [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(item) "Skyrim:Knife (item)"), [Redguard clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Clothes "Skyrim:Redguard Clothes"), a [Redguard hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard_Hood "Skyrim:Redguard Hood"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000e0dd4 "Skyrim:Boots"), and a [scimitar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scimitar "Skyrim:Scimitar"). These items would have formed a reference to [Nazir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nazir "Skyrim:Nazir"), the [Dark Brotherhood](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood") assassin.
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.
- Frossel means "frostbite" in Norwegian.
- Frossel also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Frossel "Bloodmoon:Frossel") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

## Bugs

- There are several items that you may not be able to interact with.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Frost Spirit

## Overview

| Frost Spirit (RefID: 000F82B8) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit Wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Wizard "Skyrim:Bandit Wizard") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F82B8 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F82BA |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 35-441 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 100-294 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50-150 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DraugrFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DraugrFaction "Skyrim:DraugrFaction") | | |

A Frost Spirit

The **Frost Spirit** will be encountered in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") during the quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus"). It is found in a room with a blue-glowing ice crystal. Approaching the crystal will spawn the spirit.

## Related Quests

- **[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")**: Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

# Skyrim:Frostflow Abyss

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Uncover the tragic events inside [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Entering the [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse") |
| Location(s): | [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse"), Frostflow Abyss |
| Reward: | [Sailor's Repose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sailor%27s_Repose "Skyrim:Sailor's Repose") |
| ID: | dunFrostflowAbyssQST |
| Suggested Level: | 18 |
| Difficulty: | Medium |

What happened in [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse")?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Enter the [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").
2. Investigate the lighthouse living areas and read the family's journals.
3. Retrieve the [cellar key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Mani's Cellar Key") from the burial urn on the mantle.
4. Search for the remaining family members in Frostflow Abyss.
5. Kill the family's attackers.
6. Take [Habd's remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Remains "Skyrim:Habd's Remains") to the lighthouse brazier.

### Frostflow Lighthouse

|  |
| --- |
| ***We finally did it. We bought the lighthouse. I thought Habd was just making idle promises all these years, what husband doesn't want to promise their wife the two moons from the sky, but I didn't think we'd actually manage to get it! Now if I could only find where we put everything.*** |

When you least expect it

On the snowy tundra between [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") and [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") stands [Frostflow Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse"), a remote building overlooking the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). It has been abandoned until recently, when a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") couple, Habd and [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"), finally managed to realize their dream of purchasing it, planning to spend their silver years in the lighthouse. The couple brought their two grown children, [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") and [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani"), hoping that eventually they'd decide to stay with their parents. Both children hated the place, but the parents kept hoping they would just stay in the lighthouse for a few years before venturing out into the world on their own.

As you approach the lighthouse, a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") will block your path, hinting that something went terribly wrong inside. As you enter you will be met with the sight of a dead body lying in the center of the main chamber. A broken table and the bloodstained remains of a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), primitively killed with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), are near the fireplace. The quest will immediately initiate and some strange scratching noises will appear from somewhere below. The dead body turns out to be the mother of the family, [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"), impaled by a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe"). She carries her husband's [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Habd's Journal"); read through it and you will discover what happened to Ramati and how Habd managed to kill the chaurus before venturing into the cellar for his children.

### The Scratching Sounds

|  |
| --- |
| ***Oh gods poor Ramati. It must have come out of the cellar. I'm going down there and locking the door behind me to make sure they don't escape. I don't know if I'll make it out, but I have to save my family!*** |

The mantle

From Habd's journal, it is clear that the intruders are located downstairs, but the cellar door is locked, so ignore the scratching sounds and investigate a bit further. Start in the northeastern bedroom where Habd and Ramati's double bed is positioned in the center of the room. On the end table sits [Ramati's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ramati's Journal") so read through it for some more observations and a few clues. Head into the neighboring room to the northwest, belonging to [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani") and [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi"), and follow the trail of blood to Mani's bed. Underneath the bed is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Knapsack "Skyrim:Containers") with a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Mani's Letter") where he claims not to be responsible for the odd noises coming from the basement, and how he will leave the lighthouse as soon as Habd returns from his venture into town. On a table in the same room is Sudi's [journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sudi's Journal"). Read through the last section of the journal and compare it to the last section of Ramati's journal, and you will know where the cellar key is hidden.

Head to the fireplace and investigate the burial urn sitting on the mantle. It contains the [cellar key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Mani's Cellar Key") so grab it and loot the lighthouse for valuables, including a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")* in the parents' bedroom. Finally approach the cellar door and prepare for a very long trek into the depths beneath the lighthouse, where you will find out what happened to the other family members, Sudi, Mani, and Habd.

Head down the stairs and avoid the [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") laid out by Habd in an attempt to stop the supposed skeevers. Follow the trail of blood down to a snowy chamber where two [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") will attack, effectively solving the mystery of the scratching sounds. Dispose of them both and keep an eye on the blood in the snow. Halfway through the room, the trail stops, and in front of you is a knocked-over set of shelves. Where the shelves used to stand is a huge hole in the stone wall. Proceed into the tunnel behind the wall and enter [Frostflow Abyss](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Lighthouse#Frostflow_Abyss "Skyrim:Frostflow Lighthouse").

### The Blind Dead

|  |
| --- |
| ***I don't know how long we've been down here. Father came down to find us, but those things captured him as well. I asked him if he'd seen Mother or Mani, but I don't know if he could even hear me. One of those big bugs bit him when he tried to get free and now he's feverish.*** |

Mani

Sudi

Head down the slope and discover the recognizable tents usually inhabited by the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). Before long, a Falmer will attack, along with another chaurus. The trail of blood starts again here, leading towards a plateau between the tents. Here, you can find the remains of [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani"), skewered by a [Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword") and roasting on two fires, obviously on his way to become the meal for the inhabitants of the crypt. Locate the gate to the southeast and head up the slope for another battle against a Falmer and a chaurus. Take the narrow tunnel to the southeast and beware the [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") triggering the [slicer](/wiki/Skyrim:Slicer "Skyrim:Slicer") in the ceiling.

Before long you will land in a nest filled with cobwebs and inhabited by a Falmer and two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Kill them all and proceed through the southwestern tunnel until you reach another chamber, divided into two levels, with a patrolling Falmer on the ledge above, and another on the ground. Fight them both and investigate the cage along the western wall. In there, you will find [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") lying dead in a pool of her own blood. A [scrawled page](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrawled_page "Skyrim:Scrawled page") is nearby, detailing how far her father managed to get into the cave before he was finally overpowered by the poisonous inhabitants. Sadly, a [bloodstained note](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstained_note "Skyrim:Bloodstained note") in her hand explains how she was able to commit suicide before she suffered the same fate as her father, explaining the blood and the [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") sticking out of her wrist.

### Entering the Nest

|  |
| --- |
| ***They took Father. There had been some others they brought down but they led them off and all we heard were the screams and now Father is gone too. I don't know where he was hiding it, but I think I know why he left me this dagger.*** |

The blind dead

The Reaper

Locate the slope to the southeast and proceed to the area above and fight any remaining Falmer. The only available path is located to the west and marks a point of no return, as you will be unable to get back up. When you drop down, kill the chaurus and examine the Falmer tent for a couple of useful healing potions. Then head forward through the tunnel until you reach yet another point of no return, a large chamber filled with several chaurus enemies, spitting poison at you while you slowly climb down to the bottom using the stones sticking out of the wall. The room is flooded with water and all of the walls are covered in egg sacks filled with [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"). A total of four chaurus will attack. Kill them and proceed through the tunnel to the northwest until you find yourself in another huge chamber filled with eggs and more chaurus.
With the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") DLC there are four chaurus cocoons, the third from the left will contain a [chaurus hunter fledgling](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter_Fledgling "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter Fledgling"). Locate another slope and another narrow tunnel in the northeastern corner, leading to even more egg sacks, more chaurus, two more chaurus cocoons (with one releasing another chaurus hunter fledgling as you approach) and more fights.

As the amount of egg sacks slowly increases and covers the surroundings, prepare for the final battle in the northeastern chamber where a huge [chaurus reaper](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Reaper "Skyrim:Chaurus Reaper") resides, sitting on an island surrounded by egg sacks. Pick the fight with the giant chaurus and keep an eye on your health at all times, as several smaller chaurus will join their leader. Once the reaper is dead, the quest will end, although you still haven't found the head of the family, Habd.

Open up the chaurus reaper and you will find [Habd's remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Remains "Skyrim:Habd's Remains") inside, along with his [lighthouse key](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Lighthouse_Key "Skyrim:Habd's Lighthouse Key"). Claim the key and the remains, head up the slope and loot the boss-leveled Falmer chest, then head through the narrow northeastern tunnel until you fall down in the very first chamber of the crypt.

### Last Wishes

|  |
| --- |
| ***I know they think their father will live forever, but I see his age creeping into his eyes.  He made me promise again that when he died I would put his bones in the lighthouse fire so he could look out over the ocean forever.*** |

Forever at peace

Head northwest and you will be back in Frostflow Lighthouse, with only one thing to do for the family of Redguards, namely to follow Habd's last wishes, as written in his wife's journal. Unlock the wooden door adjacent to the cellar door and travel all the way up to a ladder that leads to the very top of the lighthouse, with the impressive view described by Sudi in her journal. Habd's key will unlock the chest up there, so claim another reward and then head up the wooden ladder to the lighthouse brazier and activate it. Habd's remains will then be placed in the brazier, fulfilling his last wishes, to look out over the ocean forever. This gesture earns you the [Sailor's Repose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sailor%27s_Repose "Skyrim:Sailor's Repose"), a permanent effect causing all [healing spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration#Spells "Skyrim:Restoration") to cure 10% more.

## Notes

- If you practice [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy"), the Frostflow Abyss is an incredible source of [Chaurus Eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), with 525 guaranteed samples (516 from egg sacs and 9 hand-placed). As well as [Glowing Mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), with 96 guaranteed samples.
- Using the [Animal Allegiance](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Allegiance "Skyrim:Animal Allegiance") shout makes this quest incredibly easy to complete since it will cause every [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") in range (including [chaurus reapers](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Reaper "Skyrim:Chaurus Reaper")) to become harmless and attack other chaurus that remain hostile to you. Any chaurus under the effect of Animal Allegiance can also easily be killed with sneak attacks.

## Bugs

- If you clear Frostflow Abyss before the quest is started, you won't be able to actually finish the quest.
  -  Using the console and typing `setstage dunFrostflowAbyssQST 90` may complete this quest and remove it from your Miscellaneous Quests.
- On approaching the lighthouse, some followers may refer to it as a cave, saying *"Hmm. Caves. Wonder what's below."*
- Followers won't go past chaurus gates in the cave.
  - Bumping them (running into them to push them in a direction) or the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to push them past the gates works. Also, closing and re-opening the gates often gets followers to try again and to go through.
- The quest's Sailor's Repose reward has an incorrect taper duration set, in addition to also having an incorrect magnitude set. Its abilities are applied by perk and the effect entries are merely to make it show up in the UI when you get it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The quest may break if you pick the lock on the basement door before you've been given the notification that the quest is active.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The door will now require the key in order to proceed so that the quest doesn't completely break.

## Quest Stages

| Frostflow Abyss (dunFrostflowAbyssQST) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 5 |  | *Objective 5:* Find the source of the murders in Frostflow Lighthouse |
| 100 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 7, 10, 20, 21, 22, 90, 95.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage dunFrostflowAbyssQST stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest dunFrostflowAbyssQST`.

Frostflow Lighthouse

**Frostflow Lighthouse** is a lighthouse west-southwest of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") containing [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), and [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). It contains two zones: *[Frostflow Lighthouse](#Frostflow_Lighthouse)* and *[Frostflow Abyss](#Frostflow_Abyss)*.

A [Redguard](/wiki/Lore:Redguard "Lore:Redguard") family recently bought the lighthouse. The purchase was a long-held dream for [Habd](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd "Skyrim:Habd") and his wife [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"); however, their children [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") and [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani") weren't as keen on the move.

## Related Quests

- **[Frostflow Abyss](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Abyss "Skyrim:Frostflow Abyss")**: Uncover the tragic events inside Frostflow Lighthouse.

### Exterior

It is on a headland overlooking the coastline between [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") and [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). It is southeast of an [Imperial camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp") and southwest of [Hob's Fall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Hob%27s_Fall_Cave "Skyrim:Hob's Fall Cave"). As you approach the lighthouse, you will encounter a dead [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse") lying on the path near the entrance, while in front of the entrance is a cart holding a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison") and a [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") branch with two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") concealed underneath it. There are also a couple [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bushes around the building, a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") bush next to one of the snowberry bushes, a covered well near a single-stalled stable, and a small vegetable patch containing six [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and four [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") plants. There is a small novice-locked shed on the side of the lighthouse with a [bucket](/wiki/Skyrim:Bucket "Skyrim:Bucket") next to it. The shed itself contains a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a [broom](/wiki/Skyrim:Broom "Skyrim:Broom"), and a [pitchfork](/wiki/Skyrim:Pitchfork "Skyrim:Pitchfork") on the left and a set of shelves on the right holding a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [basket](/wiki/Skyrim:Basket "Skyrim:Basket"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on the bottom, and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on top. There is also a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") just northeast of the vegetable garden.

### Frostflow Lighthouse

As soon as you enter the lighthouse, you will see that something is very wrong. There are blood splatters on the floor, and the circular room in front of you has been turned upside-down, with a human corpse and the body of a dead [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"). On either side of you are wooden doors; one is expert-locked, while the other is master-locked. You can hear another chaurus moving around nearby. As you approach the body of [Ramati](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati "Skyrim:Ramati"), a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostflow_Abyss "Skyrim:Frostflow Abyss") will initiate directing you to find the source of the murders. Ramati is carrying [Habd's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Habd's Journal") and has a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe") sticking out of her. There are six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on the floor next to a chair. Against the wall to the northwest is a large fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and the body of a chaurus beside it with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") sticking out of it. There is a bottle of Nord mead on the floor, while on the mantlepiece is a [torchbug in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Torchbug in a Jar"), a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"). Inside the urn is [the key](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Cellar_Key "Skyrim:Mani's Cellar Key"), which opens the master-locked cellar door. If you read the family's journals (see notes), they will lead you to this key.

In the middle of the room near Ramati's body is a broken table and three overturned chairs with three [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and three [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") now on the floor. Against the east wall is a sideboard with a basket containing [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") underneath and a salmon steak, two [salt piles](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), and three fillets of [salmon meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Meat "Skyrim:Salmon Meat") on top. Above the sideboard, hanging from the ceiling are two racks holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), three [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"), and a [garlic braid](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"). To the right is a wooden table with three [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins on top. Against the wall to the southwest is a cupboard holding clutter with a bottle of Nord mead on top.

There are two open doors leading to two bedrooms from the circular room. The bedroom on the left contains two unowned single beds, one in the western corner that appears to have been Sudi's, and the other in the eastern corner that must have been Mani's. Between these are two sets of shelves back-to-back. Under Sudi's bed is a medium coin purse and a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*. On the shelves facing the bed are ten [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), a set of [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), two pairs of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), a small coin purse, a [silver necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), an [amethyst](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), a copy of *[The Legend of Red Eagle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Legend_of_Red_Eagle "Skyrim:The Legend of Red Eagle")* and another book. Beside the shelves is a small square wooden table with [Sudi's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sudi's Journal") on top. Under Mani's bed is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") and a bottle of Nord mead. Inside the knapsack are a few [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Mani's Letter") to his sister explaining that he is leaving as soon as father returns, a random [ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring "Skyrim:Ring"), some raw food, a set of [Hammerfell garb](/wiki/Skyrim:Hammerfell_Garb "Skyrim:Hammerfell Garb"), and a common book. On his set of shelves is a set of common clothes, a pair of boots, an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"). There is also a dresser against the southeast wall containing more clothes.

The bedroom on the right contains an unowned double bed coming out from the northeast wall, with an end table on either side. The one on the left has [Ramati's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ramati's Journal") on top, while the one on the right has two common books on top. Behind the door, against the southeast wall is a dresser with a copy of the [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mystery of Talara, v 2](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_v_2 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, v 2")* along with a common book on top. Against the northwest wall is a table with two common books and seven gold coins on top, and beside this is a cupboard holding some clothes, a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), two [potions of resist cold](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Cold "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Cold"), and a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"). To the right, against the northeast wall is a small set of shelves holding various clothes, [hats](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat"), and boots.

The expert-locked door to the northwest opens to reveal a flight of stairs leading up. Halfway up, a small coin purse sits on the small shelf by the wall. At the top, there are several bales of straw, a large pile of firewood, and a ladder leading to the lighthouse's exterior and brazier. Outside, there is a large locked chest that cannot be picked (it requires a key) and another ladder leading up to the side of the brazier to allow it to be lit. Back inside, the master-locked door to the east opens at the top of stairs leading down to the cellar. There are two bear traps on the stairs, the latter halfway down beside a pile of food sacks. At the bottom there are plenty more blood splatters on the floor and a large pile of firewood with a woodcutter's axe beside it. Two chaurus are wandering around the cellar, and by a stone pillar are two fish barrels with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on one of them and a pole suspended between this and the next pillar holding four whole salmon. Against the outer wall to the southwest is a pile of crates and a couple barrels, with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and an iron dagger under a basket on a crate and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the ground beside them. On the far side of the second pillar is an adept-locked chest containing minor loot. Continuing around the cellar's outer wall, to the south is a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), and to the left is a set of shelves holding a [bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt") on top, some clothes, and a sack of food. Farther left, past a food barrel is a second set of shelves holding more clothes, more food sacks, and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). To the left of this is a pile of crates, and left again are a couple knocked-over cupboards with a hole where the Falmer broke through. To the left of the hole, against the internal wall are a pile of straw bales, some crates with two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a food sack on top, and two more suspended poles holding a total of eight whole salmon.

Exiting the cellar through the hole dug by the Falmer, there is a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe") on the ground to the right. After a few paces, you proceed to *Frostflow Abyss*.

### Frostflow Abyss

The abyss contains Falmer, chaurus, and frostbite spiders, and if you have *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* installed, you will also have to deal with a few leveled [chaurus hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter") that are hidden in [cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon"). The abyss has high numbers of both [chaurus egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs") and [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), totaling up to 516 egg sacs and 93 mushrooms that can be harvested. You continue descending an icy tunnel. At the bottom, blood splatters are on the ground, and the passage opens into a cavern with two Falmer tents opposite, with a leveled Falmer magic-user in the one on the right. To either side of the tunnel you are exiting are stacks of crates, an empty chest, and barrels. On a crate to the left are five gold coins with a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") beside it. Between the stacks is a bear pelt on the ground, while off to the right is a chaurus near a gated exit, a [Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword") on the ground, and a knapsack in the corner. Around the corner to the left is a third Falmer tent, which contains a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"). The next tent is empty, while between the first two tents is the body of [Mani](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani "Skyrim:Mani") pierced by a Falmer sword and lying on a flat-topped rock with fires by his head and feet. The third tent has a small fire in front and only contains the Falmer magic-user. The exit is through the gate to the right.

Beyond the gate, the passage climbs and turns to the northeast at the top, with nine patches of [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungus at the corner. It then opens into a cave with a Falmer and a chaurus. In this area, there are several flat-topped rocks with various items on top. On the first rock on the left are one random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), two loose chaurus eggs, a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a sample of [ice wraith teeth](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith_Teeth "Skyrim:Ice Wraith Teeth"), a sample of glowing mushroom, a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, and two random potions of healing. On a rock by the east wall are two Falmer war axes, a [Falmer shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield"), a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow"), and two pieces of [chaurus chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin"). On a rock beside the wall to the southeast is a dead chaurus and a piece of chaurus chitin. To the southwest is a passage marked by a lit [torch](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") thrust into the snow on the right. Take care, as there is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that triggers a [claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw") trap from above.

At the next corner, where a sample of glowing mushroom is on the ground, the passage turns northwest and opens into a cave with a Falmer tent opposite and cobwebs and spider egg sacs to the right. Inside the tent is a leveled Falmer, and two [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") are off to the right. The passage exits this cave to the southwest, in front of the tent. The next turn is to the southwest, where there is a two-tiered cavern ahead containing two leveled Falmer and a leveled chaurus. One of the Falmer is standing at the front of the ledge above, while the other is farther back out of sight, and the chaurus is on the ground level behind the pillar in front. There is a Falmer tent on the left with a couple loose chaurus eggs on the ground in front and a novice-locked Falmer chest and two loose [skeever tails](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever_Tail "Skyrim:Skeever Tail") inside. Opposite the tent against the west wall is a pen with a closed gate, behind which is the body of [Sudi](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi "Skyrim:Sudi") with a [scrawled page](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrawled_page "Skyrim:Scrawled page") and a [bloodstained note](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodstained_note "Skyrim:Bloodstained note") on the ground beside her along with a lit torch. It is implied by the note that she used her [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") to kill herself rather than let herself be eaten alive.

Chaurus lair

Under the ledge is a pillar with a chaurus hidden behind it. On the right is a caved-in section with gaps you can look through into a cavern farther ahead. The passage continues to the southeast. As it climbs, you pass through another mushroom farm with several patches of white cap fungus. The passage brings you out on the ledge above, where there are three Falmer tents. The first tent on the right contains an apprentice-locked Falmer chest. The second tent is empty, and has several more white cap fungus patches and a Falmer war axe and a poison by a rock to the left. The third tent is to the left, and contains four loose chaurus eggs and a Falmer sword and shield. To the west is a ledge you will need to drop down to continue. Your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") (if you have one with you) may not jump down, but instead wait for you on the higher level. To prevent this, you can nudge them over the edge by running into them or using the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

There is another Falmer tent on the right and a leveled chaurus in front. Once you descend you will have no way of returning back the way you came and will have no choice but to continue. The tent contains a Falmer bow, two random potions of healing and two random poisons. This is the area you could see through the cave-in. There is an unlocked chest beside the tent, and the passage continues to the northwest. After a short distance, the passage turns again to the southwest by some more white cap fungus patches, and after a few paces ends at another ledge with two chaurus below you among many chaurus egg sacs. The cavern at the bottom has shallow water covering the floor and a passage leading northwest.

Follow this passage to the next cavern, where two chaurus, at least one of which is leveled, and several chaurus cocoons are among many more chaurus egg sacs. There is a ledge at the rear of the cavern, and the passage exits to the north. At the end is a ledge you have to drop down again into a final huge cavern with three chaurus nearby and several more coccoons around the area. There is a torch and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") in this room. To the northeast is the biggest chaurus reaper you will have seen, along with a couple smaller ones. This is the final battle. Inside the reaper are [Habd's remains](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Remains "Skyrim:Habd's Remains") and [a key](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Lighthouse_Key "Skyrim:Habd's Lighthouse Key") which unlocks the chest found at the top of the lighthouse. There is an earthen ramp climbing up to the left, which then follows the cavern walls and loops around the cavern counterclockwise. Near the top are two more empty Falmer tents and an unlocked boss leveled chest to the right of a final passage heading northeast to a drop that brings you back to the first cavern by the knapsack. Take Habd's remains up to the brazier at the top of the lighthouse to gain the active effect [Sailor's Repose](/wiki/Skyrim:Sailor%27s_Repose "Skyrim:Sailor's Repose"), which makes healing spells stronger by curing 10% more.

## Notes

- There is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") northeast of the lighthouse.
- Three journals can be found within the first floor of the lighthouse:
  - [Habd's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Habd%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Habd's Journal") can be found on the corpse of his wife, Ramati.
  - [Sudi's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Sudi%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Sudi's Journal") can be found on a table in the room to the left.
  - [Ramati's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ramati%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ramati's Journal") can be found on an end table in the room to the right.
- [Mani's letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Mani%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Mani's Letter") can be found in the knapsack in the room to the left, mentioning his intention to leave.
- If you have a follower with you, they may give the "approaching a cave" dialogue due to the lighthouse having the keyword "dungeon".
- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- On approaching the lighthouse, some followers may refer to it as a cave, saying *"Hmm. Caves. Wonder what's below."*
- Followers won't go past chaurus gates in the cave.
  - Bumping them (running into them to push them in a direction) or the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") shout to push them past the gates works. Also, closing and re-opening the gates often gets followers to try again and to go through.
- The quest's Sailor's Repose reward has an incorrect taper duration set, in addition to also having an incorrect magnitude set. Its abilities are applied by perk and the effect entries are merely to make it show up in the UI when you get it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- Some Chaurus Egg Sacs may be difficult or impossible to harvest in Frostflow Abyss.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Due to the fact that Ramati, Mani, and Sudi are part of [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") crime faction, should you resurrect and re-kill them, then you could theoretically receive a bounty in that hold.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.6, fixes this bug.
- The quest may break if you pick the lock on the basement door before you've been given the notification that the quest is active.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The door will now require the key in order to proceed so that the quest doesn't completely break.
- Two Falmer may be stuck in their tents in Frostfall Abyss.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.7, fixes this bug.
