Frostfruit Inn

**Frostfruit Inn** is a tavern and popular gathering point in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead"). It is located in the center of town, between [Rorik's Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorik%27s_Manor "Skyrim:Rorik's Manor") and [Cowflop Farmhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Cowflop_Farmhouse "Skyrim:Cowflop Farmhouse").

[Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki") tends the counter, buying and selling [food and drinks](#Standard_Merchandise) and renting out rooms for 10 gold. It consists of one area only, *[Frostfruit Inn](#Frostfruit_Inn)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") [Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Dawnguard Novice Hakar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Novice_Hakar "Skyrim:Dawnguard Novice Hakar")\* |

**\*** If he survives the related [random encounter](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Dawnguard_Novice_Hakar "Skyrim:World Interactions").

## Related Quests

- **[In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need")**: Find a [Redguard woman](/wiki/Skyrim:Saadia "Skyrim:Saadia") who is on the run from [her past](/wiki/Lore:Taneth "Lore:Taneth").
- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)")**: Find and deliver some forged documents to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Erik the Slayer](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik_the_Slayer_(quest) "Skyrim:Erik the Slayer (quest)")**: Help [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") become an adventurer.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Mralki's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are restocked every two days.

| Count | Item |
| --- | --- |
| 7 | Random [drinks](/wiki/Skyrim:Food#Beverages "Skyrim:Food") |
| 10 | Random inn [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") |

## Frostfruit Inn

Inside Frostfruit Inn

Like many other taverns in smaller settlements, Frostfruit Inn consists of a huge taproom with a fireplace in the center and the counter in the opposite end of the room from the entrance. Several wooden tables are scattered around, all of them set with food and drink. In addition to the taproom, the inn also has three smaller rooms with a total of four owned beds, one of them reserved for paying customers.

To the right of the front door, in the southern corner, is the first table which is dressed with two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), some [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), a [goat cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), some [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), and one bottle each of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). In the corner stands a single food barrel, while two similar barrels can be found in the adjacent corner to the east. Next to the barrels are another table with two loaves of bread, and more wine and alto wine, two bottles of each. The next table contains exactly the same. The last table along the northeastern wall holds three loaves of bread, a bottle of wine and two of alto wine. Next up is a set of shelves with four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), two [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), five bottles of wine and four of alto wine. Additionally, the shelves also holds seven bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). The last table for paying customers can be found between the entrance door and the nearest room, which can be used by either [Mralki](/wiki/Skyrim:Mralki "Skyrim:Mralki") or [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik"). The table has two [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and, in a basket on the floor, three [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg").

The bar takes up most of the northwestern part of the taproom and Hralki can be found behind the counter 24 hours a day. On display is some [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Hidden on the shelves underneath the bar are five gold coins, a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), three [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), eight bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of wine and one of alto wine. There is also a basket with a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"), an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") and an [eidar cheese wheel](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"). In the northern corner is a set of shelves with two bottles of alto wine and six of regular wine, along with four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). Hanging from the ceiling, above a single food barrel, are no less than eleven dead [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant").

The room you can rent is located to the northeast and contains two beds, a dresser with random [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing "Skyrim:Clothing"), and two bottles of alto wine on top, and an empty chest. The bed you can rent is the one in the northern corner. Adjacent to this room are two even smaller rooms, both of them located to the southwest. The room on the left contains a wardrobe with clothes, a chest with minor loot, and a bottle of [Black-Briar Mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead"). The room to the right belongs to [Erik](/wiki/Skyrim:Erik "Skyrim:Erik") and contains a dresser with clothing and a chest with minor loot.

## Notes

- Although a conversation between Mralki and Erik talks about a downstairs, the inn has no basement.
  - Despite this, the chest that is also mentioned in the conversation does exist, albeit unused, in the game's files.

# Skyrim:Frostmere Crypt

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Nordic Ruin.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Nordic_Ruin.png) | Nordic Ruin: Frostmere Crypt ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Frostmere+Crypt)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Frostmere_Crypt "Lore:Frostmere Crypt")) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | Never (storage is [safe](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Safe_Locations "Skyrim:Containers")) |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| [The Pale Blade](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Blade "Skyrim:The Pale Blade") *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| FrostmereCryptExterior01, FrostmereCryptStart, FrostmereCrypt01, FrostmereCryptWorld01, FrostmereCryptWorld02 | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| South-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") East-northeast of [Stonehills](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehills "Skyrim:Stonehills") | |
| Special Features | |
| [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") | [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") |
| # of [Grindstones](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") | 1 |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |
| # of [Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") | 2 |
| # of [Corundum](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") | 2 |
| # of [Silver](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") | 1 |
| # of [Orichalcum](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") | 1 |

Frostmere Crypt

**Frostmere Crypt** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and the unique wispmother the [Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)"). It contains two zones: *[Frostmere Crypt](#Frostmere_Crypt)* and *[Frostmere Depths](#Frostmere_Depths)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in Frostmere Crypt.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Stairs lead up to the entryway, where an empty pot hangs over a firepit. To the right is a broken sideboard with a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and a pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top. To the right of this in the corner is an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). To the right of the door leading inside are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack, and to the left is a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). Outside the entrance a short distance to the west are two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). On the snowy hill behind the dungeon, you can find another ruined book, and a dead [Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr").

### Frostmere Crypt

Upon entering, you will be at the top of a flight of stairs; if you are sneaking, you will be able to overhear two bandits discussing [Eisa](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa_Blackthorn "Skyrim:Eisa Blackthorn") and the stolen sword. There is a stone table immediately on your left as you enter holding a random war axe, a random healing potion, and some ruined books. There are also four sacks under the table, and an unusable barrel and a chair opposite. Taking the stairs down past three more unusable barrels on your right and a pile of firewood on your left, the passageway opens into a room containing two bandits, with plenty of sacks, crates, boxes, and barrels around the room. On the left is a stone table with two chairs, where the bandits are sitting. On the table are three sacks, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and *[Kyr's Bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr%27s_Bounty "Skyrim:Kyr's Bounty")*. To the left of the table is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). There is a gated path ahead, and an open gate on the right; through this doorway will come another bandit, who will probably be alerted when you attack the first two.

In the room to the right are more crates, sacks, and barrels, and an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the right of the chest is a set of shelves containing copies of *[The Song of Pelinal, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v7 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v7")*, *[The Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Oblivion_Crisis "Skyrim:The Oblivion Crisis")*, and *[A Dance in Fire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v1 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v1")*, a ruined book, a skull, a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), some random armor, and two sacks. To the right of the shelves is a table and a chair with a small window looking out into the first room. On the table is a copy of *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*.

Back in the first room, to the left of the gated passageway is a pull chain that opens it. The passageway leads down some stairs and turns to the west; you will hear talking ahead, and pass a large urn on your left. Just past this is a junction with a turn to the south, and an iron door straight ahead that is barred from the other side. There is a lit brazier on your right at the junction, with a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") on top. There is an end table on the left just after the junction, with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top.

Taking the left turn at the junction, you can see a covered raised walkway ahead, with a table and chair where it turns. On the table is a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a copy of *[Palla, volume 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Palla,_volume_1 "Skyrim:Palla, volume 1")*. The walkway is in a room with three levels. You can see a bandit down on the middle level guarding a lever. Following the covered walkway east to a passageway running north-south, there are a couple cages ahead, with blood splattered up the wall. To the left (north) as you enter the passageway is a bandit guarding an adept-locked door; he is to the right of the door, and can be quite hard to see. To the left of this door is a chair and a set of shelves holding several ruined books, and copies of *[The Ransom of Zarek](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ransom_of_Zarek "Skyrim:The Ransom of Zarek")*, *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")*, and *[The "Madmen" of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_%22Madmen%22_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:The \"Madmen\" of the Reach")*. Behind the adept-locked door is a small storage room containing a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), three unusable barrels, two food sacks, and a set of four weapon racks. There is a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on the floor in front of the weapon racks, and a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Helmets "Skyrim:Armor") on the barrels. The racks hold an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer").

Following the passageway to the south, you will pass two sets of shelves, one on either side of the passageway. The shelves on the left hold more ruined books, a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")*, and a troll skull. The shelves on the right have various items of crockery, more ruined books, and on a plinth in front, a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*. Continue into the next room, which has two open doors on this level, as well as wooden stairs descending to a lower level where two more bandits are discussing the theft of the sword. The first room on your left appears to be [Kyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr "Skyrim:Kyr") the bandit leader's bedroom. It contains an unowned double bed with an end table to the right. On top of the end table is *[Kyr's Log](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr%27s_Log "Skyrim:Kyr's Log")*. To the right of the end table is a sideboard holding a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") and a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Reading the log will update the quest [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady"). There is also an unlocked chest, an unusable barrel, several sacks, and a chair in the room. The next room appears to be another bedroom, with a dresser by the door with a random helmet on top. There are also two bedrolls, a table and two chairs, and a crate and a food sack with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") leaning against them. On the table is *[Ra'jirr's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr%27s_Note "Skyrim:Ra'jirr's Note")* and *[Eisa's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eisa's Journal")*, which give you more info on what has happened.

Down the stairs, after dealing with the two bandits, you will find four long tables with two benches each around the room. To the east is a large fireplace, with an empty pot over it. To the right are several sacks and barrels containing food. There is a sideboard against the south wall holding a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and a bottle of [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right is a cupboard, with a couple sacks on a shelf. Hanging above the sideboard are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), a sample of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and a rabbit. There is a doorway to the north leading to a raised wooden bridge, and an unlocked wooden door to the west.

Through the door to the west is another bedroom, with a bandit sitting at a table in front of you. Behind the table is a fireplace, with a wardrobe to the left, and four bedrolls scattered around this part of the room. Farther into the room is a dresser on the right, with a copy of *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")* on top. Behind a pile of rubble is another bedroll, with another bandit sleeping. Opposite this bedroll is a small set of shelves holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some ruined books. Continuing along a passageway is a sideboard on your left, with a random healing potion on top. Just past this sideboard, through a door to the right, is the bandit guarding the lever you saw earlier. The lever operates the raised bridge. At the end of the passageway is an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus growth, with a partially buried burial urn behind.

Returning to the wooden bridge, dropping it may well have alerted two more bandits, who come to investigate. After dealing with the bandits, cross the bridge to a stone pillar, which is circled by a wooden spiral ramp leading to the bottom level. There is a sack at the bottom of the ramp, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") under the ramp. Around the room are two carts full of rubble, several pickaxes, and a long table holding a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"). There is a tunnel heading down to the west. At the bottom of the stairs, you will hear two bandits talking on the right, next to a cart. The tunnel turns to the south and continues to descend. Be careful, as there is a [falling boulder trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") at the top of the stairs. The easiest way to avoid it is to walk to the top of the stairs, and as soon as you hear it activating, stand still until it finishes. At the bottom of the stairs is a junction, with the tunnel running east-west. Opposite you at the junction is a lit brazier on the ground; to the left of the brazier is a second iron ore vein. The dead end to the east has an empty open chest, probably the one mentioned in Kyr's log as the bandits' first big discovery. Next to the chest is a pickaxe.

Taking the tunnel to the west, you pass a cart on your left, then descend more stairs. At the bottom of the stairs, the passage starts looking like a typical Nord burial site, with alcoves in the walls for corpses. The passageway runs north-south again; to the south is a bandit mining at a dead end. There is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") here on the west wall. Following the passage north, you will see another partially buried burial urn, and an iron door leading to *Frostmere Depths*.

### Frostmere Depths

Upon entering this area, you will see a forest in front of you, with Kyr dying to your right. He will try to talk to you, but apart from finding out what you already knew about [Ra'jirr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr "Skyrim:Ra'jirr") trying to take the sword back, you will learn nothing new. Once he is dead, you can loot his body. The path leads forward, and you will see [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp") floating around and Ra'jirr ahead being attacked by a wispmother named the Pale Lady. They will be fighting in front of a stone table which has a weapon stand on it, with a medium coin purse, a loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") next to the stand. The table is on a stone island, with water nearly all the way around it.

If you follow the cave wall on the left from the entrance door, you will pass under a fallen tree. There is a lootable skeleton leaning against a tree next to a leveled warhammer and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). Continuing past the skeleton and climbing slightly to the left of a stone pillar, you will find a master-locked chest at the base of a tree (near the northwest corner of the cave).

There is a stream to the right of the table. Follow the stream up to the source for an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein"). Crossing the stream, you come to a flight of stairs ascending to the northwest. Turning to your right, at the top you will see the word wall, which teaches part of the Ice Form shout. To the left of the wall is a burial urn. Past the wall is a second flight of stairs up from this level, which leads to an iron door that is a shortcut back to *Frostmere Crypt*. To the left of the door is another unlocked chest, with a random greatsword stuck in the stone to the left of the chest (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Before using the door, jump up the rock formations to the west along the wall of the cavern to reach a stream above two waterfalls, with another taller waterfall falling from near the roof above. On this natural shelf, careful searching will reveal an iron sword and three loose septims.

In this zone, you can find at least five [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), seven [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), eight [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and ten [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), as well as two [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") flying around.

Through the iron door back in the first zone is a flight of stairs, with a pressure plate at the top which triggers a dart trap from the left. You can avoid all damage by waiting on the plate until the darts stop firing. The passage then leads to a flooded room, with a bridge spanning the room, and a flight of wooden steps on the right descending into the water. Under the water there is a lot to collect, including an adept-locked chest. To the south, next to a piece of fallen stonework, is a sideboard with a leveled battleaxe and a random poison on top. Against the north wall in a semi-circular formation are two random soul gems, one filled, one empty. Finally, in the northwest corner on a broken stone table is a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). Crossing the bridge leads to an iron door barred from this side; from there, you may retrace your steps to the exit.

## Notes

- According to data in the Creation Kit, Frostmere Crypt was once named **Palemoon Crypt** instead.
- The forest section of the dungeon is considered outdoors, therefore you can fast travel from there.

## Bugs

- Approaching Frostmere Crypt from the north may not trigger the quest, [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If the quest [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") directs you here, check to see whether you have already visited this location. This location does not respawn, so if you have been here before, the Moon Amulet cannot spawn here and you cannot complete the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  -  This bug is fixed by version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").
  - You will need to reload a previous save and get a different quest location from [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- You may find the greatsword floating in the air above the chest.
  - The sword cannot be interacted with and is not affected by shouts, spells, or most attacks. However, shooting it with an arrow will drop it to the ground for retrieval.
- Using the grindstone will swing the camera past the cell and into the blue void.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. The grindstone has been moved to the center of the room.
  - Exit the grindstone, and the camera will return to normal.

Frostmere Crypt

**Frostmere Crypt** is a medium-sized [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") south-southwest of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") and the unique wispmother the [Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady_(creature) "Skyrim:The Pale Lady (creature)"). It contains two zones: *[Frostmere Crypt](#Frostmere_Crypt)* and *[Frostmere Depths](#Frostmere_Depths)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Ice Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Form "Skyrim:Ice Form") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bandit Attack](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Attack "Skyrim:Bandit Attack")**[HF](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"): Rescue your beloved from kidnappers. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady")**: Find out what happened in Frostmere Crypt.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Stairs lead up to the entryway, where an empty pot hangs over a firepit. To the right is a broken sideboard with a [ruined book](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book") and a pair of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets") on top. To the right of this in the corner is an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"). To the right of the door leading inside are two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from a rack, and to the left is a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"). Outside the entrance a short distance to the west are two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). On the snowy hill behind the dungeon, you can find another ruined book, and a dead [Vigilant of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Vigilant_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Vigilant of Stendarr").

### Frostmere Crypt

Upon entering, you will be at the top of a flight of stairs; if you are sneaking, you will be able to overhear two bandits discussing [Eisa](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa_Blackthorn "Skyrim:Eisa Blackthorn") and the stolen sword. There is a stone table immediately on your left as you enter holding a random war axe, a random healing potion, and some ruined books. There are also four sacks under the table, and an unusable barrel and a chair opposite. Taking the stairs down past three more unusable barrels on your right and a pile of firewood on your left, the passageway opens into a room containing two bandits, with plenty of sacks, crates, boxes, and barrels around the room. On the left is a stone table with two chairs, where the bandits are sitting. On the table are three sacks, two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and *[Kyr's Bounty](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr%27s_Bounty "Skyrim:Kyr's Bounty")*. To the left of the table is an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"). There is a gated path ahead, and an open gate on the right; through this doorway will come another bandit, who will probably be alerted when you attack the first two.

In the room to the right are more crates, sacks, and barrels, and an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). To the right of the chest is a set of shelves containing copies of *[The Song of Pelinal, v7](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v7 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v7")*, *[The Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Oblivion_Crisis "Skyrim:The Oblivion Crisis")*, and *[A Dance in Fire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v1 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v1")*, a ruined book, a skull, a sample of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), some random armor, and two sacks. To the right of the shelves is a table and a chair with a small window looking out into the first room. On the table is a copy of *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*.

Back in the first room, to the left of the gated passageway is a pull chain that opens it. The passageway leads down some stairs and turns to the west; you will hear talking ahead, and pass a large urn on your left. Just past this is a junction with a turn to the south, and an iron door straight ahead that is barred from the other side. There is a lit brazier on your right at the junction, with a random [greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Greatsword "Skyrim:Greatsword") on top. There is an end table on the left just after the junction, with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on top.

Taking the left turn at the junction, you can see a covered raised walkway ahead, with a table and chair where it turns. On the table is a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and a copy of *[Palla, volume 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Palla,_volume_1 "Skyrim:Palla, volume 1")*. The walkway is in a room with three levels. You can see a bandit down on the middle level guarding a lever. Following the covered walkway east to a passageway running north-south, there are a couple cages ahead, with blood splattered up the wall. To the left (north) as you enter the passageway is a bandit guarding an adept-locked door; he is to the right of the door, and can be quite hard to see. To the left of this door is a chair and a set of shelves holding several ruined books, and copies of *[The Ransom of Zarek](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ransom_of_Zarek "Skyrim:The Ransom of Zarek")*, *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")*, and *[The "Madmen" of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_%22Madmen%22_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:The \"Madmen\" of the Reach")*. Behind the adept-locked door is a small storage room containing a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), three unusable barrels, two food sacks, and a set of four weapon racks. There is a pair of random [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor") on the floor in front of the weapon racks, and a [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Helmets "Skyrim:Armor") on the barrels. The racks hold an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), and a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer").

Following the passageway to the south, you will pass two sets of shelves, one on either side of the passageway. The shelves on the left hold more ruined books, a copy of *[Thief of Virtue](/wiki/Skyrim:Thief_of_Virtue "Skyrim:Thief of Virtue")*, and a troll skull. The shelves on the right have various items of crockery, more ruined books, and on a plinth in front, a copy of the [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Red Kitchen Reader](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Red_Kitchen_Reader "Skyrim:The Red Kitchen Reader")*. Continue into the next room, which has two open doors on this level, as well as wooden stairs descending to a lower level where two more bandits are discussing the theft of the sword. The first room on your left appears to be [Kyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr "Skyrim:Kyr") the bandit leader's bedroom. It contains an unowned double bed with an end table to the right. On top of the end table is *[Kyr's Log](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyr%27s_Log "Skyrim:Kyr's Log")*. To the right of the end table is a sideboard holding a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace") and a [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"). Reading the log will update the quest [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady"). There is also an unlocked chest, an unusable barrel, several sacks, and a chair in the room. The next room appears to be another bedroom, with a dresser by the door with a random helmet on top. There are also two bedrolls, a table and two chairs, and a crate and a food sack with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") leaning against them. On the table is *[Ra'jirr's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr%27s_Note "Skyrim:Ra'jirr's Note")* and *[Eisa's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Eisa%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Eisa's Journal")*, which give you more info on what has happened.

Down the stairs, after dealing with the two bandits, you will find four long tables with two benches each around the room. To the east is a large fireplace, with an empty pot over it. To the right are several sacks and barrels containing food. There is a sideboard against the south wall holding a [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese") and a bottle of [Alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right is a cupboard, with a couple sacks on a shelf. Hanging above the sideboard are two [garlic braids](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic_Braid "Skyrim:Garlic Braid"), a sample of [dried frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Dried Frost Mirriam"), two [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), and a rabbit. There is a doorway to the north leading to a raised wooden bridge, and an unlocked wooden door to the west.

Through the door to the west is another bedroom, with a bandit sitting at a table in front of you. Behind the table is a fireplace, with a wardrobe to the left, and four bedrolls scattered around this part of the room. Farther into the room is a dresser on the right, with a copy of *[Yellow Book of Riddles](/wiki/Skyrim:Yellow_Book_of_Riddles "Skyrim:Yellow Book of Riddles")* on top. Behind a pile of rubble is another bedroll, with another bandit sleeping. Opposite this bedroll is a small set of shelves holding a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and some ruined books. Continuing along a passageway is a sideboard on your left, with a random healing potion on top. Just past this sideboard, through a door to the right, is the bandit guarding the lever you saw earlier. The lever operates the raised bridge. At the end of the passageway is an [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus growth, with a partially buried burial urn behind.

Returning to the wooden bridge, dropping it may well have alerted two more bandits, who come to investigate. After dealing with the bandits, cross the bridge to a stone pillar, which is circled by a wooden spiral ramp leading to the bottom level. There is a sack at the bottom of the ramp, and an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") under the ramp. Around the room are two carts full of rubble, several pickaxes, and a long table holding a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"). There is a tunnel heading down to the west. At the bottom of the stairs, you will hear two bandits talking on the right, next to a cart. The tunnel turns to the south and continues to descend. Be careful, as there is a [falling boulder trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") at the top of the stairs. The easiest way to avoid it is to walk to the top of the stairs, and as soon as you hear it activating, stand still until it finishes. At the bottom of the stairs is a junction, with the tunnel running east-west. Opposite you at the junction is a lit brazier on the ground; to the left of the brazier is a second iron ore vein. The dead end to the east has an empty open chest, probably the one mentioned in Kyr's log as the bandits' first big discovery. Next to the chest is a pickaxe.

Taking the tunnel to the west, you pass a cart on your left, then descend more stairs. At the bottom of the stairs, the passage starts looking like a typical Nord burial site, with alcoves in the walls for corpses. The passageway runs north-south again; to the south is a bandit mining at a dead end. There is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") here on the west wall. Following the passage north, you will see another partially buried burial urn, and an iron door leading to *Frostmere Depths*.

### Frostmere Depths

Upon entering this area, you will see a forest in front of you, with Kyr dying to your right. He will try to talk to you, but apart from finding out what you already knew about [Ra'jirr](/wiki/Skyrim:Ra%27jirr "Skyrim:Ra'jirr") trying to take the sword back, you will learn nothing new. Once he is dead, you can loot his body. The path leads forward, and you will see [wisps](/wiki/Skyrim:Wisp "Skyrim:Wisp") floating around and Ra'jirr ahead being attacked by a wispmother named the Pale Lady. They will be fighting in front of a stone table which has a weapon stand on it, with a medium coin purse, a loose [septim](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a filled random [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") next to the stand. The table is on a stone island, with water nearly all the way around it.

If you follow the cave wall on the left from the entrance door, you will pass under a fallen tree. There is a lootable skeleton leaning against a tree next to a leveled warhammer and a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"). Continuing past the skeleton and climbing slightly to the left of a stone pillar, you will find a master-locked chest at the base of a tree (near the northwest corner of the cave).

There is a stream to the right of the table. Follow the stream up to the source for an [orichalcum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein"). Crossing the stream, you come to a flight of stairs ascending to the northwest. Turning to your right, at the top you will see the word wall, which teaches part of the Ice Form shout. To the left of the wall is a burial urn. Past the wall is a second flight of stairs up from this level, which leads to an iron door that is a shortcut back to *Frostmere Crypt*. To the left of the door is another unlocked chest, with a random greatsword stuck in the stone to the left of the chest (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Before using the door, jump up the rock formations to the west along the wall of the cavern to reach a stream above two waterfalls, with another taller waterfall falling from near the roof above. On this natural shelf, careful searching will reveal an iron sword and three loose septims.

In this zone, you can find at least five [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), seven [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), eight [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower"), and ten [mora tapinella](/wiki/Skyrim:Mora_Tapinella "Skyrim:Mora Tapinella"), as well as two [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") flying around.

Through the iron door back in the first zone is a flight of stairs, with a pressure plate at the top which triggers a dart trap from the left. You can avoid all damage by waiting on the plate until the darts stop firing. The passage then leads to a flooded room, with a bridge spanning the room, and a flight of wooden steps on the right descending into the water. Under the water there is a lot to collect, including an adept-locked chest. To the south, next to a piece of fallen stonework, is a sideboard with a leveled battleaxe and a random poison on top. Against the north wall in a semi-circular formation are two random soul gems, one filled, one empty. Finally, in the northwest corner on a broken stone table is a random [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). Crossing the bridge leads to an iron door barred from this side; from there, you may retrace your steps to the exit.

## Notes

- According to data in the Creation Kit, Frostmere Crypt was once named **Palemoon Crypt** instead.
- The forest section of the dungeon is considered outdoors, therefore you can fast travel from there.

## Bugs

- Approaching Frostmere Crypt from the north may not trigger the quest, [The Pale Lady](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale_Lady "Skyrim:The Pale Lady").
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9.26.0.8, fixes this bug.
- If the quest [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") directs you here, check to see whether you have already visited this location. This location does not respawn, so if you have been here before, the Moon Amulet cannot spawn here and you cannot complete the quest.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
  -  This bug is fixed by version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch").
  - You will need to reload a previous save and get a different quest location from [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- You may find the greatsword floating in the air above the chest.
  - The sword cannot be interacted with and is not affected by shouts, spells, or most attacks. However, shooting it with an arrow will drop it to the ground for retrieval.
- Using the grindstone will swing the camera past the cell and into the blue void.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, addresses this issue. The grindstone has been moved to the center of the room.
  - Exit the grindstone, and the camera will return to normal.

# Skyrim:Frostmoon Crag

## Overview

Frostmoon Crag

**Frostmoon Crag** is a small camp under a rock overhang south of [Mount Moesring](/wiki/Skyrim:Mount_Moesring "Skyrim:Mount Moesring") and northeast of the [Abandoned Lodge](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Lodge "Skyrim:Abandoned Lodge") inhabited by [werewolves](/wiki/Skyrim:Werewolf "Skyrim:Werewolf").

The Frostmoon pack is the last true werewolf pack in Solstheim according to its leader [Majni](/wiki/Skyrim:Majni "Skyrim:Majni"), whose father and grandfather were the previous alphas. [Rakel](/wiki/Skyrim:Rakel "Skyrim:Rakel")'s parents were also pack members. Majni's brother [Akar](/wiki/Skyrim:Akar "Skyrim:Akar") isn't very sociable. [Hjordis](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjordis "Skyrim:Hjordis")'s pack was destroyed by [werebears](/wiki/Skyrim:Werebear "Skyrim:Werebear"); she remains with Majni's pack until they can help her reclaim her lands.

The pack members prefer to remain free in the wilderness. They warn non-werewolves away from their camp, but will welcome other werewolves who respect their law. They fully embrace their lycanthropy, and worship "Lord" [Hircine](/wiki/Lore:Hircine "Lore:Hircine"). Majni will offer to sell four rings blessed by their Daedric patron to a werewolf who has Hircine's favor.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Akar](/wiki/Skyrim:Akar "Skyrim:Akar")  [Hjordis](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjordis "Skyrim:Hjordis")  [Majni](/wiki/Skyrim:Majni "Skyrim:Majni") [General Goods](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "General Goods")  [Rakel](/wiki/Skyrim:Rakel "Skyrim:Rakel") |

### Miscellaneous Quests

- **[Visit the hunters at Frostmoon Crag](/wiki/Skyrim:Visit_the_hunters_at_Frostmoon_Crag "Skyrim:Visit the hunters at Frostmoon Crag")**: Talk to the hunters at Frostmoon Crag.

### World Interactions

- **[Frostmoon Invitation](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Frostmoon_Invitation "Skyrim:World Interactions")**[DB](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn")

## Frostmoon Crag

The normal approach to the crag is from the south. Partway up the slope, on the right are two [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"). At the top of the slope near the camp, you will be addressed by Rakel, who sits on a rock with a lit lantern. If you are a werewolf, regardless of whether you are currently in werewolf form, she will welcome you. You may then speak with Majni, who will offer to sell you the four rings blessed by Hircine noted below. If you aren't a werewolf, the pack members will treat you as a trespasser, and will become hostile if you loiter too long or draw your weapon.

The camp

The camp is under a rock overhang facing southeast. In the middle is a campfire with four wooden plates, two of which hold a piece of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a [pheasant breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant_Breast "Skyrim:Pheasant Breast"), and two [raw rabbit legs](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Rabbit_Leg "Skyrim:Raw Rabbit Leg"). Southwest of the fire is an unusable mead barrel, with three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and an [elixir of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Elixir of Enhanced Stamina") on the ground next to the barrel. Farther southwest are two [tanning racks](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") and a hay pile serving as bedding, with a [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and a wooden plate holding a piece of venison and a raw rabbit leg on the hay pile. Southeast of the mead barrel is a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") leaning against a wood pile. West of the fire are two more hay piles and an adept-locked chest next to a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). Northeast of the fire is the final hay pile and a large rock splattered with blood, with a [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") on the rock.

Four [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") plants grow under and near the overhang. The four hay piles and all low-value items will be free to use and take after you speak with Majni if you are welcomed by the pack.

## Notes

- A [Shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") is northwest of the cave, along with a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"), an [East Empire Pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant"), two [silver ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"), and two [sapphire geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Geode "Skyrim:Sapphire Geode").
- The four rings available for purchase from Majni are the [Ring of Bloodlust](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Bloodlust "Skyrim:Ring of Bloodlust"), [Ring of Instinct](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_Instinct "Skyrim:Ring of Instinct"), [Ring of the Hunt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Hunt "Skyrim:Ring of the Hunt"), and [Ring of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ring_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Ring of the Moon").
- If your lycanthropy is cured after you first speak with Majni, he will no longer talk with you or sell you the rings.

# Skyrim:Frostroot Cave

Frostroot Cave

**Frostroot Cave** is a cave in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"), north of [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel"). It contains the entrance to [Nchuanthumz](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz"), a Dwarven player home.

## Related Quests

- **[The Sanctuary and the Manufactory](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sanctuary_and_the_Manufactory "Skyrim:The Sanctuary and the Manufactory")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuanthumz:_Dwarven_Home "Skyrim:Nchuanthumz: Dwarven Home"): Repair a Dwarven ruin and make yourself at home.

## Exterior

The entrance to the cave is located just uphill of and behind [Kagrenzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Kagrenzel "Skyrim:Kagrenzel"), near the entrance to the latter. A [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") is located to the left of the cave entrance, and a [moonstone ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein") to the right.

[(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")

## Interior

[(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")
A snow-covered passageway leads into the icy cavern. Three bandits are present, trying to plunder the cave for its Dwemer artifacts. You will have to fight your way through them to reach Nchuanthumz.

Dead-end path with chest

A dead-end path branches off to the right about halfway down the main passage. At the end of that, on the left, is a Dwarven Chest. Continuing down the main passage, three of Artifacts' low-level hired bandits loiter about. They will attack if they detect you. There is another Dwarven chest on the right as you turn the final corner before the double doors of Nchuanthumz itself come into view. Finally, a half-buried barrel lies just left of the doorway.

## Notes

- A [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") can appear within Frostroot Cave when exiting from Nchuanthumz.

## Bugs

- Frostroot Cave is labeled as a Quick Test Cell from inside Nchuanthumz on the local map.
- Sometimes when entering Frostroot Cave, a dragon will spawn, start flying through the floor/walls and become hostile to the player.
-  When exiting Nchuanthumz into Frostroot Cave, the door is labeled Quick Test Cell.
-  The door from Frostroot Cave into Nchuanthumz will have two doors to open. The first with the generic "open door" and the second prompting entrance to Nchuanthumz.

*This [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim")-related article is a [stub](/wiki/UESPWiki:Stub "UESPWiki:Stub"). You can help by [expanding it](https://en.uesp.net/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Frostroot_Cave&action=edit).*

# Skyrim:Frothar

## Overview

"Skyrim:During sieges, staff and family hide."); [TownWhiterunFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction "Skyrim:TownWhiterunFaction") | | |

Frothar

**Frothar** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who lives in [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"). He is the eldest son of [Jarl Balgruuf the Greater](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") and brother to [Dagny](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagny "Skyrim:Dagny") and [Nelkir](/wiki/Skyrim:Nelkir "Skyrim:Nelkir"). Of the jarl's three children, Frothar is the only one who isn't rude toward you and won't make any condescending remarks.

Like the jarl's other children, he spends all his time inside Dragonsreach. He wakes up at 6am and stays in the children's room in the Jarl's Quarters talking with his siblings before heading out to play in the main hall at 9am. He spends his whole day wandering in the hall, taking an hour long lunch at 12pm and a two hour long dinner at 5pm. After dinner, he heads back to his room then waits until 10pm to go to sleep for eight hours.

Frothar wears red [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and a small amount of gold.

## Dialogue

:   *"Father says I'm too young to train with a sword, so I practice with my fists."*
:   *"Hope this war lasts long enough that I get to fight in it. Battle! Glory!"*
:   *"You're not from around here. I'll bet you're here to help with the war!"*

If spoken to after the completion of [The Fallen](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Fallen "Skyrim:The Fallen") but before you begin [The World-Eater's Eyrie](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie"):

:   *"Is it true? Did you really capture a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing") on the Great Porch?"*

## Conversations

His sister, Dagny, will sometimes complain to him about a new dress:

**Dagny**: *"I'm so angry, I can hardly stand it! Father promised me a new dress days ago, now where is it?"*
**Frothar**: *"It takes a while to make a dress, Dagny. You have to be patient."*
**Dagny**: *"But I don't want to be patient! I want my dress right now! Father promised!"*
**Frothar**: *"All you ever do is complain about what you want. You're a spoiled baby."*
**Dagny**: *"I'm going to tell father you said that. He'll tan your hide for sure!"*

## Notes

- If Whiterun is conquered by the Stormcloaks, then Frothar's father moves to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") but he does not. Also, his dialogue does not change.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. He will move to the Blue Palace.

## Bugs

- Frothar will try to sleep in his sister [Dagny](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagny "Skyrim:Dagny")'s bed instead of his own. This behavior is due to him being assigned the wrong sleep package.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- He also can be found in front of the [Whiterun stables](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Stables "Skyrim:Whiterun Stables"), just standing there no matter the time of day or night, and answering generic child greetings when talked to.

# Skyrim:Frozen Fish

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Catch arctic fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | 300 Gold |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ3 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain") [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | **Next →** [Darkest Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Depths "Skyrim:Darkest Depths") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain") [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") | | → Next | [Darkest Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Depths "Skyrim:Darkest Depths") | | |

[File:SR-quest-Frozen Fish.jpg](/w/index.php?title=Special:Upload&wpDestFile=SR-quest-Frozen_Fish.jpg "File:SR-quest-Frozen Fish.jpg")

Frozen Fish

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Receive a Fishing Work Letter from a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier").
2. Travel to [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") and speak with [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water").
3. Read the list of arctic fish.
4. Obtain a [Cod](/wiki/Skyrim:Cod "Skyrim:Cod").
5. Obtain an [Arctic Grayling](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Grayling "Skyrim:Arctic Grayling").
6. Obtain an [Arctic Char](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Arctic Char").
7. Obtain an [Angler Larvae](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Larvae "Skyrim:Angler Larvae").
8. (Optional) Read [Fishing Mastery, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v3 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v3").

## Detailed Walkthrough

Fish tank after completion of the quest

To begin this quest, speak to Swims-In-Deep-Water in the Riften Fishery:

:   **I got your letter. I'm ready for the next fishing challenge.**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*
:   **Alright. I'll be back with the fish.**

He then hands you a [list of arctic fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Arctic_Fish "Skyrim:List of Arctic Fish"), which tells you that you need to catch:

- [Angler Larvae](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler_Larvae "Skyrim:Angler Larvae") - You will need to use the Alik'ri rod. Multiple are guaranteed to spawn in [Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench") on the ocean floor.
- [Arctic Char](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Char "Skyrim:Arctic Char") - Use the Argonian rod at an Arctic spot. Can also be found at [Hela's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Hela%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Hela's Folly"), [Orphan's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Orphan%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Orphan's Tear") (within the sunken deck) and Pilgrim's Trench.
- [Arctic Grayling](/wiki/Skyrim:Arctic_Grayling "Skyrim:Arctic Grayling") - Use the Argonian rod at an Arctic spot.
- [Cod](/wiki/Skyrim:Cod "Skyrim:Cod") - Use the Argonian rod at an Arctic spot. Can also be found outside [Anga's Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Anga%27s_Mill "Skyrim:Anga's Mill") and outside [Bronze Water Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bronze_Water_Cave "Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave").

You can also optionally pickup a copy of [Fishing Mastery, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Mastery,_v3 "Skyrim:Fishing Mastery, v3") from the shelf in the backroom.

Once you have the fish required return to Swims:

:   **Here are the fish you asked for.**
:   *"It has done a good thing. It will take this gift as a token of gratitude."*

He will then reward you with 300 gold.

## Notes

- [Crustacean Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Crustacean_Extermination "Skyrim:Crustacean Extermination") is the prerequisite of this task, as it will reward you [Alik'ri Fishing Rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Items#Alik.27ri_Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Items").
  - It is not required to wait for the Courier to deliver the letter. Upon completion of Crustacean Extermination, you can head straight to Swims-In-Deep-Water and immediately request the next quest. If the Courier was already headed your way, this will make him behave as if he already delivered the letter to you.

## Bugs

- This quest may attempt to remove a courier note from his container even if it isn't present because the quests were done in a different order.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Frozen Fish (ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ3) | | |

| 10 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me another fishing challenge. I should read the list he gave me to see what I will need to catch. |
| 20 |  | The fish that Swims-In-Deep-Water has tasked me with catching are commonly found in the freezing waters of Skyrim's snow-capped landscapes. Once I've caught one of each, I should return them to him. I can consult the third volume of Fishing Mastery to learn more about my quarry. |
| 21 |  | I have read the third volume of Fishing Mastery. All of the fish I need to catch to complete the challenge can be caught at fishing spots wherever there is freezing water near snow and ice. The docks of Windhelm, the water near Dawnstar, and the small lake near Nightgate Inn were mentioned as places I could try casting my line. |
| 200 | ☑ | I've given Swims-In-Deep-Water all of the fish he requested as proof of completing his fishing challenge. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ3 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ3`.

# Skyrim:Fruki's House

## Overview

|  |

Fruki's House

**Fruki's House** is a small house in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), and the residence of [Fruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki "Skyrim:Fruki"). It is located north of [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Fruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Fruki "Skyrim:Fruki") |

### Exterior

It is at the farthest edge of town next to [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine"), facing the bay on the opposite side from [Silus Vesuius's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Silus_Vesuius%27s_House "Skyrim:Silus Vesuius's House"). In front is the jetty that [The Sea Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Sea_Squall "Skyrim:The Sea Squall") is moored at and next to the house is the [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") that the miners use. There are steps leading up to an enclosed deck in front of the house. The rocks and snow pile up quite close to the rear of the property.

### Fruki's House

Fruki's house

On your left upon entering there is a single owned bed in the eastern corner. In the middle of the southeast wall is a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel next to a tall wardrobe with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") atop, which contains only minor loot. Another single owned bed is in the southern corner, with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") by the foot of the bed. There is a fireplace opposite the door on the southwest wall with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the hearth. To the left of the fireplace is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"). To the right of the fireplace is a long wooden table and bench. On the table are several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") and an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"). In the northern corner of the room is a square wooden table and two chairs. On this table is another pickaxe, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two bottles of Nord mead, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and five loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

## Notes

- The *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")* describes the building as follows:

:   *"Fruki and [Land](/wiki/Skyrim:Lond "Skyrim:Lond"), the miners working the Quicksilver veins, live here in this small structure in which Fruki was raised. They occasionally speak with [Borgny](/wiki/Skyrim:Borgny "Skyrim:Borgny") and [Edith](/wiki/Skyrim:Edith "Skyrim:Edith"), who take the other shifts to keep the mine productive— when [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf") isn't running the operation into the ground."*

## Overview

Fruki at work

**Fruki** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [miner](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner_(class) "Skyrim:Miner (class)") who works in the [Quicksilver Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Mine "Skyrim:Quicksilver Mine") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar").

She carries her [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Fruki%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Fruki's House"), and a random selection of [lower-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Poor "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She wears a set of [miner's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Miner%27s_Clothes#00080697 "Skyrim:Miner's Clothes") with [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0009cca1 "Skyrim:Boots").

She wakes up every morning at 7am and prepares breakfast using her [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"). At 8am she walks the short distance to the neighboring Quicksilver Mine where she spends twelve hours in the dimly lit tunnels, tirelessly mining ore for her boss [Leigelf](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf "Skyrim:Leigelf"). At 8pm, she goes to the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn") for a bit of socializing with the townsfolk before her bedtime at midnight. The only exception to this routine is when you first enter Dawnstar; she will then be inside Windpeak Inn, discussing the strange [nightmares](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") with [Erandur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur"), [Irgnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Irgnir "Skyrim:Irgnir"), and [Thoring](/wiki/Skyrim:Thoring "Skyrim:Thoring").

## Dialogue

Before you have completed [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare"), Fruki will say:

:   *"[Lady Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") will save us from these nightmares. You'll see."*

Like most of the miners in town, Fruki almost exclusively talks about her work. She might also mention the feud between her boss and his ex-wife [Beitild](/wiki/Skyrim:Beitild "Skyrim:Beitild"):

:   *"Used to be twice as many miners working here before all this trouble started."*

:   *"I work in the mine, just like everyone else."*

### Conversations

When you first enter Dawnstar, you'll find her engaged in a conversation in the Windpeak Inn.

:   **Irgnir:** *"It's a curse! It has to be! I've got to get out of this town."*
:   **Fruki:** *"Irgnir, get a hold of yourself. They're just dreams. Please tell her, Erandur."*
:   **Erandur:** *"Listen to your friend, Fruki. They are just dreams, my dear. I assure you that it is quite normal."*
:   **Irgnir:** *"It's the same dream over and over again. You think that's normal? It's evil I tell you!"*
:   **Fruki:** *"Erandur, she has a point. You keep telling us no harm will follow these dreams, but they must be an omen."*
:   **Thoring:** *"Give him a chance to speak. He's trying to help us."*
:   **Erandur:** *"Everyone, please. I'm doing what I can to end these nightmares. In the meantime all I ask is you remain strong and put your trust in Lady Mara."*
:   **Irgnir:** *"I... I will. Thank you..."*

Even though they work in competing mines, Fruki can often be seen talking to Irgnir at the Windpeak Inn.

:   **Irgnir:** *"You should quit working in the Eastern Mine. Leigelf's no good to work for."*
:   **Fruki:** *"Leigelf is a good man, and I'm not running out on him now."*
:   **Irgnir:** *"Oh, got a bit of an interest in your boss do you?"*
:   **Fruki:** *"No, not that it's any of your business."*

:   **Irgnir:** *"Tough day at the mines. I swear the ore is getting harder to dig."*
:   **Fruki:** *"You're just getting older."*
:   **Irgnir:** *"That's why I come here to talk to you. You're all heart."*

# Skyrim:Frykte Peak

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Frykte Peak ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Frykte+Peak)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2POIChest01 | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| Just west of [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch") Northeast of [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow") | |

Frykte Peak, seen from Saering's Watch

**Frykte Peak** is one of the highest points on Solstheim, near [Saering's Watch](/wiki/Skyrim:Saering%27s_Watch "Skyrim:Saering's Watch"). The marker for this peak does not appear on the compass until you have [climbed](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") nearly to the top.

Frykte Peak is easiest to reach with a [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse")—using [Summon Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Summon_Arvak "Skyrim:Summon Arvak")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is recommended. It is reachable on foot with enough persistence, but requires some creative jumping. See [this article](/wiki/Skyrim:Mountain_Climbing "Skyrim:Mountain Climbing") for tips on mountain climbing.

## Notes

-  The `tmm` command won't make it visible on the map.
- *Frykte* is the Norwegian word for *to fear*.

# Skyrim:Fugitive

## Overview

| Fugitive | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Voice Type | [MaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCommoner") | | |

Fugitive

A hunter fires an arrow at a fugitive

The **Fugitive** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") who can be [randomly encountered](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Hey_you_there.2C_take_this "Skyrim:World Interactions") in the wilderness. He will give you an item—which is usually enchanted—on sight. He will tell you not to reveal his location and flee. A [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") will appear later, asking you if anyone has come by. You have the options to lie to him and to deny that there was anyone or to tell him where the fugitive has gone or to give him the item, for 1 gold, which isn't very profitable. For the highest profit you may choose the second option, letting the hunter kill the fugitive and then loot his body.

Similar to other [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit#One-Handed_Melee "Skyrim:Bandit"), his equipment includes leveled [light armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Light Armor (item)"), a leveled one-handed weapon and shield. He also carries a random selection of items that bandits have with them.

## Dialogue

The fugitive will run up to you, saying:

:   *"Take this and hold onto it. I'll be back for it later. I'll pay you good. Don't lose it."*
:   **Umm...** or **Slow down. Explain yourself.**
:   *"No time to talk. Snitch or double-cross me and I'll kill you. I mean it!"*

Afterwards, he will try to avoid the hunter.

## Notes

- Despite what the fugitive says, there are no repercussions, regardless of whether you snitch on him or what you do with the item.
- If you kill the fugitive before the hunter arrives, he will still tell you that he plans to kill the now-dead thief.
- Due to the fugitive lacking a crime faction, you will not gain a bounty for any crime committed against him.
- The item he gives you won't be tagged as "stolen", allowing you to sell it.
- If you don't respond to his dialogue options, he will leave, telling you to let him know if you see the fugitive again.

## Bugs

- The fugitive may approach and talk to you if you are in [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form"). **?**
- If you drop the item the fugitive gave you before the hunter runs and speaks to you, you can still tell him about it for 1 gold, then retrieve it. **?**
- The hunter may spot the fugitive and attack him immediately, without letting him talk to you first. **?**

# Skyrim:Fultheim the Fearless

## Overview

This article is about the Nord in the Abandoned Shack. For the Nord at the Nightgate Inn, see [Fultheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Fultheim "Skyrim:Fultheim").

| Fultheim the Fearless (RefID: 0002E3F1) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Abandoned Shack](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_Shack "Skyrim:Abandoned Shack") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0002E3F1 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0002E3E8 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 1 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Class Details | [CombatWarrior1H](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleNord](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleNord") | | |

Fultheim the Fearless

Fultheim unmasked

**Fultheim the Fearless** is one of the three hostages in the [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") quest. He is a Nord mercenary who works out of Skyrim. He bears no particular ills against any person, but when asked about his potential assassination, he reasons that as a sellsword, any number of people could have put a contract out on him as he has been proven to be too difficult to kill through battle. When intimidated, he admits to sometimes getting carried away during battle.

Fultheim wears [scaled armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Armor"), [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots"), and [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Bracers "Skyrim:Scaled Bracers"), along with an [execution hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Execution_Hood "Skyrim:Execution Hood").

Despite his name, he is quite afraid while he is being held captive. He fights back tears and begs for his life, insisting that he is just a soldier who follows orders. He also thinks that somebody might pay to have him killed because he slaughtered sleeping people, which he thought was immoral.

## Related Quests

- **[With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...")**: Repay your debt to [the Family](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Brotherhood "Skyrim:Dark Brotherhood"), and show you are willing to kill on command.

## Dialogue

When approached for the first time, he will say:

:   *"What did I do? Please, whatever it is, I'm sorry."*

At other times, he will tell you one of the following:

:   *"I... I can hear you talking out there. Please, let me go. I've done nothing to you."*
:   *"Is this about that raid last week? I told Holgrim there was no honor in killing sleeping men, but he wouldn't listen! It wasn't my fault, I swear!"*
:   *"I'm just a soldier. Killing is my job! Surely you can't fault a man for doing his job?"*
:   *"Please, oh please, I don't want to die..."*

If you kill one of the other captives and then approach Fultheim, he will cry out:

:   *"Oh, gods, please! Let me live! I'll do anything you want!"*

You can ask him a few questions before making your choice.

:   **Who are you?**
:   *"My name is Fultheim. I'm a soldier. Well, mercenary, really. You know, a... a sellsword. I've lived in Skyrim all my life.
    That's all! I'm a nobody, really. So can't you just let me go?"*
:   **Would someone pay to have you killed?**
:   *"What? Oh gods, I don't want to die..."*
:   **Answer me, or die! (Intimidate)**

    :   *"Please! I don't know! I mean, I'm a soldier. I've killed people. When I was ordered to. Maybe there were some times... some times I got carried away?
        But war is war. Right? Nobody could blame me for that. Could they?"*
:   **Shhh... Don't be afraid. You can tell me. (Persuade)**

    :   *"Okay, well... I guess it's possible. I've been selling my sword arm for years now. Killed a lot of people. Could be someone wanted revenge. But... But you're not going to kill me. Right?"*

Upon death, Fultheim will scream,

:   *"Aiiiieee!"*

[Astrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Astrid "Skyrim:Astrid") will comment on his fate, depending on who else has been killed:

:   *"Oh ho. The whimpering Nord, eh? Yes, yes, I can see how you'd come to that conclusion. Interesting choice."*
:   *"The timid warrior and the [sly Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Vasha "Skyrim:Vasha"). Must have been one or the other, right?"*
:   *"The blubbering barbarian and the [tenacious mother](/wiki/Skyrim:Alea_Quintus "Skyrim:Alea Quintus"). Must have been one of them, right?"*
:   *"Well, well, aren't we the over-achiever? Three possibilities, three victims. Must have been one of them, right? So why take chances..."*

Should you choose to kill Astrid, you can approach Fultheim, who will beg you to untie him, saying:

:   *"Please... Please! Release me! Cut my bonds!"*

If you do, he will be immensely grateful.

:   *"Thank you! Thank you! I'll never speak of this to anyone, I promise!"*

Any time after his release, he can be found, repeating his promise:

:   *"Thank you! Thank you! I won't tell anyone what happened here, I swear it!"*
