Geirmund's Hall

**Geirmund's Hall** is a small [Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Ruins "Skyrim:Nordic Ruins") east of [Ivarstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Ivarstead "Skyrim:Ivarstead") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"), and the draugr [Sigdis Gauldurson](/wiki/Skyrim:Sigdis_Gauldurson "Skyrim:Sigdis Gauldurson"). It contains only one zone, *[Geirmund's Hall](#Geirmund.27s_Hall)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend")**: Investigate the forgotten [Gauldur Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends").
- **[Caught in the Rain](/wiki/Skyrim:Caught_in_the_Rain "Skyrim:Caught in the Rain")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Catch rainy weather fish.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Fishing camp

The ruin is on an island in the middle of [Lake Geir](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Geir "Skyrim:Lake Geir"). Several [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") and [red mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"), two [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root") plants, a [thistle](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle "Skyrim:Thistle"), a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue"), and [gourds](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") grow on the island. Several upright stones and three patches of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus are in front and on either side of the entrance. Two [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") are just east of the entrance, and one [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is a short distance to the northwest. Near some rocks to the north are two patches of [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") fungus.

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found to the northeast, along with a [fishing rod](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Rod "Skyrim:Fishing Rod"), drying [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and [brook bass](/wiki/Skyrim:Brook_Bass "Skyrim:Brook Bass"), two [cooked brook bass](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Brook_Bass "Skyrim:Cooked Brook Bass"), [cooked carp](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Carp "Skyrim:Cooked Carp"), a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Knapsack "Skyrim:Containers"), a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and copies of *[Line and Lure](/wiki/Skyrim:Line_and_Lure "Skyrim:Line and Lure")* and *[Horker Attacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Attacks "Skyrim:Horker Attacks")*. Fish from [temperate lakes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") can be caught here.

### Geirmund's Hall

Upon entering, there are many fungi growing in the cave, including fourteen bleeding crown, nineteen [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), and five [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"). Two skeevers will attack as you descend toward a large sinkhole. To the west of the hole is a [dead adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer "Skyrim:Adventurer") who is carrying a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")*, which will start the quest [Forbidden Legend](/wiki/Skyrim:Forbidden_Legend "Skyrim:Forbidden Legend") if you haven't already started it. The only other item of interest is an iron ore vein on your left as you descend.

Jump down through the hole into the pool below. Under the pool you will find an [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and a short dead-end passage containing a [burial urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn"), and at the end, an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword"), a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), a random [potion of waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing"), and a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") on the sandy bottom. Be careful to make sure your [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") does not come with you, because you may be unable to leave the water-filled passage and drown when they block your exit. There is an iron door to the west, with wooden stairs leading up to it out of the water. Opposite, among some rubble, is a burial urn and a large coin purse.

#### Spiderweb Hall

Through the door you will face two frostbite spiders in a web-filled room, with an adept-locked door to the north and a passage to the south. Behind the door is a short passage with a broken table on your right holding a random set of [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"), a random [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Shield "Skyrim:Shield"), and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing").

#### Flooded Catacombs

At the start of the passage to the south is an adept-trapped chest on a dresser, and next to this is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that triggers a [poison dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from the walls ahead. Continuing to the west down a flight of stairs into some shallowly flooded catacombs with [rotating pillars](/wiki/Skyrim:Spinning_Symbol "Skyrim:Spinning Symbol"), look at the symbols on the walls.

The order is **Eagle—Whale—Snake—Whale**. There are pillars for each symbol in this area guarded by one [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") each, at least one of which is a magic-user. Halfway through the pillar section, there is a table with a random filled soul gem on a [weight sensitive plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Weight_Sensitive_Plate "Skyrim:Weight Sensitive Plate"), which will set off a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") in the form of a mammoth head and tusks swinging down from the ceiling. You can set the trap off safely if you are beside or on top of the table when you take the soul gem. There is also a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on the table. There is a burial urn by the first rotating pillar, another burial urn (partially buried) farther along the wall on the same side, and diagonally opposite a large [urn](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") by the table. At the bottom of the stairs is the first pillar (**Eagle**). Turning right, the second pillar (**Whale**) is next to the stairs. The third pillar (**Snake**) is behind the table. Going slightly backwards, then left, you can see the fourth pillar (**Whale**). Then turn to the right and pull the lever so you can go through the door to the north.

#### Lord Geirmund's Tomb

Archmage Geirmund

A short tunnel with several more fungi growing along it leads to an area where you will encounter three more draugr: one at the bottom of the ramp, and two more guarding the corpse of [Geirmund](/wiki/Lore:Geirmund "Lore:Geirmund") at the top. Care should be taken, as fighting these three can alert another leveled archer draugr on a walkway above the room. There is a well-hidden large coin purse in the second shelf of the fallen bookshelf at the base of the ramp; only the very top of it shows through the sand. A second hidden large coin purse is among some rubble to the southwest. To the west is a sideboard with a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and a single [arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") on top. To the right is a set of shelves holding [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

Before approaching Geirmund for the key, you can use a [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") or skillful jumping to reach the broken bridge on the west side of the room, leading to a [leveled](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") treasure chest. Be careful when opening the door, as it is [rigged](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable"): there is a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that shoots [firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") at you directly behind it. Remove the soul gem to disarm the trap. You can stand to the side to avoid the blast, or disarm the tension cable first. The chest itself is not trapped, but does have an expert-level lock.

Proceed to take the key from Geirmund's skeleton (the key is visible in his hand, but it's not in his inventory). You can grab the [epitaph](/wiki/Skyrim:Geirmund%27s_Epitaph "Skyrim:Geirmund's Epitaph") for some content reference if you want, and Geirmund has some pretty good loot for the taking. To the east of Geirmund is an urn, with an unlit brazier in front containing a random [mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace "Skyrim:Mace"). The key will open the door directly behind Geirmund's resting place, or you can pick the adept lock.

#### Crafty Passage

As soon as it opens, a draugr may or may not spawn at the [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") table, and there is a large frostbite spider or skeever to the left. Up the stairs to the right, there is a random [potion of invisibility](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Brief_Invisibility "Skyrim:Potion of Brief Invisibility") and an urn. On the table with the enchanter is a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") and a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), while near the table on the ground is a random empty soul gem. Once you've dispatched the frostbite spider or skeever, proceed to the west past two bookcases, the second of which has a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") on top. At the bottom of the stairs on the ground to the right is a small coin purse. Proceed up the stairs, where another leveled draugr will be patrolling. There is another sideboard on the left, with a potion, a random pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor#Boots "Skyrim:Armor"), and a random bow on top.

Once you reach the drawbridge, you'll be facing the raised bridge (with another draugr behind it, if you didn't deal with it from below) and a lever. There will be spear holes in the wall pointed in your direction; the said lever is a dummy that activates this [spear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spear_Trap "Skyrim:Spear Trap"). Instead of that lever, if you are facing the bridge, the lever that will actually lower the bridge is directly behind you, hidden in the corner. (If you did not Whirlwind Sprint or jump up to the hidden treasure chest from before, you can now simply drop off the right side of this bridge to reach it, then backtrack here once you've gotten the treasure.)

Kill the draugr here, and cross the bridge to the center pillar. Here lies another lever that will drop the other side of the bridge. Two more draugr are roaming around the far side of this walkway. You can easily shoot and kill them before dropping the bridge. However, when they die, they may land on the pressure plate behind them, setting off the [swinging axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") in the hallway. You will find one more draugr, a magic-user, just past the pressure plate, around the corner at the end of that hallway. The chain to deactivate the axe trap is found here on the wall. After you descend the following stairs, you will pass another sideboard with a random poison on top. Around the corner, the passage ends on a ledge.

#### Sigdis Gauldurson's Tomb

Sigdis' sarcophagus

This next area is where you'll confront the boss, Sigdis Gauldurson. The area below the ledge where you will fight the boss is full of many more of the fungi already found throughout the ruin, while many hanging moss also grow in this area. Once you drop down here and head toward the quest objective, Sigdis Gauldurson will burst out of his sarcophagus. Don't waste arrows/magic/shouts while he is rising, as they will not harm him, and may trigger a bug (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

#### Boss Strategy

Sigdis will conjure two illusions of himself and teleport to one of four spots in the room. The illusions will die in one hit, so find the real one and defeat him. There are several strategies to do this:

- The illusions glow with a faint blue aura, while Sigdis himself does not; Sigdis also wears a helm with horns curling downward (similar to an [Ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord#Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord")), while the illusions have helms with horns pointing upward or no horns. Equip your bow and arrow, crouch behind his tomb for cover, and aim for the one without the glowing blue aura and with the telltale helm. If you destroy the two illusions, Sigdis will teleport and create them again.
- If you approach Sigdis, he will generally try to deal one more hit of damage before teleporting and summoning new illusions. This rapid room-crossing can be tricky to overcome for melee-dependent classes. For melee players, a crushing shield bash will stagger him long enough to land an overpowered hit or two quick follow-up hits before he teleports away; attacking Sigdis directly with a melee weapon may cause it to be disarmed. Otherwise, summoning magic and ranged spells may prove useful. For example, [Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Bane of the Undead") will both damage Sigdis and eliminate the illusions.
- Return to the ledge from which you entered the cavern. It's then easy to pick off Sigdis, and he doesn't seem to shoot back, although he still teleports himself and his two minions around the room.
- While Sigdis is teleporting, put a rune on one of the spots where he appears, then quickly turn to aim at another spot. When he finishes teleporting, either you will have hit him, or you've eliminated an illusion. If the latter, quickly fire again at another spot, and you can potentially eliminate two of the three possible versions of him.
- Once you've hit the real Sigdis, his damaged health bar will start to show when your sight hovers over him, while the illusions will never show a damaged health bar, as they dissipate when damaged. This is an easy way to tell where Sigdis is when he teleports.

Once Sigdis is defeated, loot his corpse for the [Gauldur Blackbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur_Blackbow "Skyrim:Gauldur Blackbow"), a *[Writ of Sealing](/wiki/Skyrim:Writ_of_Sealing_(Sigdis) "Skyrim:Writ of Sealing (Sigdis)")*, and a [Gauldur Amulet Fragment](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauldur_Amulet_Fragment "Skyrim:Gauldur Amulet Fragment") (a quest item for Forbidden Legend). You'll find an escape tunnel behind his sarcophagus leading to a treasure room, featuring a boss-level unlocked chest with a plate holding two pearls and a small pearl. To the right is a set of shelves holding a random helmet, gauntlets, and shield, a soul gem, a random potion of magic, and a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Words and Philosophy](/wiki/Skyrim:Words_and_Philosophy "Skyrim:Words and Philosophy")*. To the south, a passage leads to a lever that will open a hidden door back to the first room.

## Notes

- Tell any followers to wait outside the cavern or on the tomb side of the boss room, out of harm's way. Do not leave them on the islands in the middle of the water, as they may die or kill Sigdis' clones, making your task harder.
- If the key is not on the altar, look on the floor, as the draugr above on the landing may attack you with shouts and knock it off.
- Sigdis' clones have petty souls. You can farm the respawning clones using a bow with a [soul trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Trap_(effect) "Skyrim:Soul Trap (effect)") enchantment and a decent [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") skill until your soul gems are all filled. However, the only way to leave the ruin is through the secret door that opens when you kill Sigdis, so you can only exploit this mechanism for a single session.
- Sigdis' clones can be used to easily gain Vampire Lord perks.
- Geirmund's Hall also [appears](/wiki/Online:Geirmund%27s_Hall "Online:Geirmund's Hall") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- Save before falling down the hole. Sometimes the pillars won't turn when activated. Reloading may resolve this.
- There's a repeating clanking sound coming from the wall in the upper parts of the stairs up to the hallway with the drawbridge lever, and in parts of the hallway itself. The source of the sound is at the top of the stairs, after the room with the arcane enchanter, caused by a potion partially stuck in the wall continuously spawning and falling every few seconds. It can't be picked up.
- Followers caught in the pendulum trap room sometimes disappear for good. **?**
- If you get a kill move on Sigdis and he teleports while in the middle of the move, his body may disappear, making it impossible to complete the quest.
  -  The body can be recovered with the console. Type `prid 000A5E68`, then `moveto player`, then `disable`, then `enable`. This will make the body accessible again.
- Do not attempt to use [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") against Sigdis while he is emerging from his coffin. He will glitch, and you will be unable to kill him. **?**
  - If you do glitch him by starting with Unrelenting Force, you may be able to "fix" him by using the shout again on the "dead body" while fighting him. One of the three spawns during the fight will almost always be a dead body.
- If you are knocked down by Sigdis' Unrelenting Force shout, you may get stuck behind the wooden bars at the southeastern end of the water area. **?**
- If you knock Sigdis down with your Unrelenting Force shout before but not during his teleporting state, his AI may break and he will not attack for the rest of the fight. **?**
- If you kill Sigdis before he teleports, the exit may not open, and you will be trapped.
- If you paralyze Sigdis before he disappears, he will glitch and be unkillable.
- You may be unable to loot Sigdis if he has been disintegrated. **?**
- The dungeon may not appear as clear on your map once Sigdis is defeated. **?**

# Skyrim:Get Outfitted

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Get a free set of Imperial armor.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") |
| Location(s): | [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") |
| Reward: | Imperial Armor |
| ID: | CW01AOutfitImperial |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion") | | |

*"Light, medium, or heavy?"*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") after clearing out [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad").
2. Go to [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand").
3. Pick Heavy, Medium, or Light Imperial armor.

### You're In the Army Now

After successfully clearing the [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") from [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"), your usefulness has been proven to [Legate Rikke](/wiki/Skyrim:Legate_Rikke "Skyrim:Legate Rikke"). Your oath has been sworn; you are officially an Imperial soldier and protector of the Empire. It's time you look the part. [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") tells you to go to [Beirand](/wiki/Skyrim:Beirand "Skyrim:Beirand"), the [smith](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Blacksmith "Skyrim:Solitude Blacksmith"), to get outfitted with your own [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"). Talk to Beirand and choose your preferred weight:

| Armor Type | Helmet | Boots | Shield | Bracers | Armor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Heavy | Imperial Helmet | Imperial Boots | Imperial Shield | Imperial Bracers | Imperial Armor |
| Medium | Imperial Light Helmet | Imperial Light Boots | Imperial Shield | Imperial Light Bracers | Studded Imperial Armor |
| Light | Imperial Light Helmet | Imperial Light Boots | Imperial Light Shield | Imperial Light Bracers | Imperial Light Armor |

When you are properly outfitted, Beirand will admonish you: *"Now, that's it. One free outfit per soldier. You lose that, or get it banged up, you'll need to pay like everyone else."*

## Notes

- It is not possible to do this quest if you first join the legion by giving the [Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Jagged_Crown "Skyrim:Jagged Crown") to General Tullius.
- Note that the Medium option contains one heavy armor piece (shield) and the rest are light armor pieces.
- Although Beirand tells you that you'll need to pay if you lose or damage the Imperial armor set he gave you, you can forge a new set yourself.
  - [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch") 1.9 makes it possible to forge Imperial Light Armor.
- After the completion of this quest, Beirand is no longer [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs#Beirund "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- Beirand's inventory will carry less items after this quest.[*verification needed — see [talk page](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Get_Outfitted)*]

## Bugs

- If you join the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") (either [initially](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Joining the Stormcloaks") or by defecting after [The Jagged Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Jagged_Crown_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Jagged Crown (Imperial)")), this quest is never shut down which leaves Beirand in a perpetual essential alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Get Outfitted (CW01AOutfitImperial) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | *Objective 1:* Get Imperial gear from Beirand |
| 255 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 11, 12.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage CW01AOutfitImperial stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest CW01AOutfitImperial`.

# Skyrim:Gharol's Message

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Dreamshadow](/wiki/User:Dreamshadow "User:Dreamshadow"), [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), checked by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029")  **Reward**: written by [Beezer1029](/wiki/User:Beezer1029 "User:Beezer1029"), *not checked* |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Deliver [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol")'s sword to [Lash](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol") |
| Location(s): | [Burguk's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Burguk's Longhouse"), [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") |
| Reward: | Leveled gold |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol")) |
| ID: | FreeformDushnikhYalA |

*An Orc blade is a very personal thing. Anger, regret, pride.*

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol") at [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal").
2. Deliver the sword to [Lash gra-Dushnikh](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh") at [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten").

### A Mother's Pride

Gharol is a [blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Skyrim:Blacksmith") living in [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal"), the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). If you're permitted to enter the stronghold, you may talk to her about her weapon business. She will tell you that while she occasionally trades with the outside world, Orcs infuse their weapons with their private emotions: *"An Orc blade is a very personal thing. Anger, regret, pride. All these things are put into our steel."* In the conversation you will discover that Gharol's daughter, [Lash](/wiki/Skyrim:Lash_gra-Dushnikh "Skyrim:Lash gra-Dushnikh"), chose to leave the stronghold, breaking with [Orc custom](/wiki/Lore:Orc "Lore:Orc") and bringing shame and grief to her mother. Gharol tells you that she has forged a sword to channel her feelings about her daughter's betrayal, and to send her daughter a message. Then she will ask you to honor her with a task: bring the sword to her daughter in [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten"); Lash will know what it means.

### Message Received

Travel to Karthwasten and deliver the sword to Lash. She will reply, *"So that's it, then. 'Don't come back.' Thank you. Here. You honored my mother's task and should be rewarded."* The forsaken daughter will reward you with leveled gold and ask you to leave her alone.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.

- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformDushnikhYalA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformDushnikhYalA`.

# Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Decide the fate of a [heretical cult](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Temple "Skyrim:Tribunal Temple").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading [Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional](/wiki/Skyrim:Heretic_Dossier:_Blacksmith%27s_Confessional "Skyrim:Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional") at the Temple in Raven Rock. |
| Location(s): | [Raven Rock Temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple "Skyrim:Temple"), [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz"), [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear") |
| Reward: | [Hand Ethra Mavandas](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Ethra_Mavandas "Skyrim:Hand Ethra Mavandas"), [Hand Kydren Indobar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kydren_Indobar "Skyrim:Hand Kydren Indobar"), [Vesparth the Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Vesparth_the_Toe "Skyrim:Vesparth the Toe") and [Watchman Sindras](/wiki/Skyrim:Watchman_Sindras "Skyrim:Watchman Sindras") as followers, [Tribunal Armory Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Armory_Key "Skyrim:Tribunal Armory Key"), ability to craft [Her Hand Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Hand_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Her Hand Armor Set") and [Indoril Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin#Indoril_Armor "Skyrim:Chitin") |

| --- | |
| |  |  |  | | --- | --- | --- | |  | **Concurrent** [Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)"), [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware"), [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"), [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs") | **Next →** [Ashen Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Heart "Skyrim:Ashen Heart") | | |

A cult of Almalexia worshippers is operating on Solstheim

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read [Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional](/wiki/Skyrim:Heretic_Dossier:_Blacksmith%27s_Confessional "Skyrim:Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional") at the Temple in Raven Rock.
2. Travel to [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") Forge.
3. Kill [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan").
4. Travel to Ashfall's Tear.
5. Talk to [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") and start three new tasks [Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs"), [Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation"), [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware").
6. Complete three new tasks above.
7. Return to Ashfall's Tear and clear the temple from [Ash Zombies](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Zombie "Skyrim:Ash Zombie") attacking
8. Talk to [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") and get [Tribunal Armory Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Armory_Key "Skyrim:Tribunal Armory Key")

## Detailed Walkthrough

Fahlbtharz Forge and the heretic

The ALMSIVI puzzle

To begin this quest, read the [Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional](/wiki/Skyrim:Heretic_Dossier:_Blacksmith%27s_Confessional "Skyrim:Heretic Dossier: Blacksmith's Confessional") at the Temple in Raven Rock. It can be found on a table in the first room on the right on the lower floors of the temple.

You will then have to travel to [Fahlbtharz](/wiki/Skyrim:Fahlbtharz "Skyrim:Fahlbtharz") and enter the Forge. Inside you will find [Hand Kenro Hlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro_Hlan "Skyrim:Hand Kenro Hlan"), he will be hostile and you will have to kill him. Once he is dealt with, search his body to find a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kenro%27s_Note "Skyrim:Hand Kenro's Note"), unenchanted weapon, [Kenro's Helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Kenro%27s_Helmet "Skyrim:Kenro's Helmet") and [Kenro's Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Kenro%27s_Robes "Skyrim:Kenro's Robes"). Picking up these items will also start [Trueflame (quest)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)").

You will then need to head to [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear"), once inside you will find a ALMSIVI puzzle. The correct order for the stone pillars is ASV.

If you decide to wear Kenro's helmet and robes and infiltrate the temple ranks, the ordinators at the door will not be hostile, however, if you are not wearing these, they will attack on sight.

### Joining the Heretics

If you disguise yourself, you can peacefully talk to [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") and either persuade or prove yourself by fighting Almalexia's Hands:

:   **I'm actually not one of your followers. But I'd still like to join your ranks.**
:   *"You expect me to believe that?"*

    :   **I could prove my loyalty by praying to the Goddess. (Persuade).**
    :   *"Okay, okay, you've talked me into it."*
    :   **If I bested your warriors in combat, it would show the Goddess favors me.**
    :   *"How can I argue with that?"*

If you manage to persuade her you will have to pray at the nearby Shrine of Almalexia next to the large statue at the temple entrance. Doing so acts as praying at any other shrine, curing diseases and replacing any active blessing with Almalexia's Blessing. This blessing grants +10 to the Heavy Armor skill and +10% damage with One-Handed weapons for 8 hours. Once you've prayed at the shrine, you've joined the heretics and can continue on to the next stage of the quest.

If you want to prove yourself through combat, you will have to fight [Hand Kydren Indobar](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Kydren_Indobar "Skyrim:Hand Kydren Indobar") until he submits, then [Hand Ethra Mavandas](/wiki/Skyrim:Hand_Ethra_Mavandas "Skyrim:Hand Ethra Mavandas"), [Watchman Sindras](/wiki/Skyrim:Watchman_Sindras "Skyrim:Watchman Sindras") and finally [Vesparth the Toe](/wiki/Skyrim:Vesparth_the_Toe "Skyrim:Vesparth the Toe"). After this you will need to speak to Drevlan again:

:   **I've won the combat trial. I trust this means I have her favor?**
:   *"The deed is done. We need speak of it no longer."*

After this point, you are now accepted. You are free to switch back to your other apparel if you want. Speak to Drevlan again to continue.

:   **I await the Goddess' command. Her word is our law.**
:   *"You speak the truth."*

    :   **Does the Goddess have a task for me?**
    :   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*

She will then hand you a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Masks_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Masks of the Tribunal") detailing your task and the location of the other masks. Reading the note will begin three quests:

- **[Her Word Against Theirs](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Word_Against_Theirs "Skyrim:Her Word Against Theirs")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Spread the word of the Goddess [Almalexia](/wiki/Lore:Almalexia "Lore:Almalexia").
- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").
- **[Careless Curation](/wiki/Skyrim:Careless_Curation "Skyrim:Careless Curation")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Find the missing Curate to retrieve the [Mask of Sotha Sil](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Sotha_Sil "Skyrim:Mask of Sotha Sil").

Ash zombies

Once you return to the temple you will have to clear out the ash zombies that are attacking the temple, once they are dealt with you will need to speak to the Matriarch:
[(?)](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data")

She will reward you with the [Tribunal Armory Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Tribunal_Armory_Key "Skyrim:Tribunal Armory Key"), ability to craft [Her Hand Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Her_Hand_Armor_Set "Skyrim:Her Hand Armor Set") and [Indoril Armor Set](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin#Indoril_Armor "Skyrim:Chitin") is also gained, it requires [Elven Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven#Elven_Smithing "Skyrim:Elven") perk.

### Destroying the Heretics

If you decide to destroy the heretics, you can disguise yourself still in order to speak to Matriarch Drevlan, or you can just deal with them the traditional way.

If you choose the traditional way, you will have to first fight the two [ordinators](/wiki/Skyrim:Ordinator "Skyrim:Ordinator") that guard the first door into the temple.

You will then have to fight everyone gathered in the ritual room past the statue. There is a narrow straight tunnel before the room. It is possible to fight everyone in the room one on one at this choke point.

You will still be able to complete the other Ghost of the Tribunal Quests by looting the bodies for notes. There is no key to the armory however and this prevents you from obtaining Skullcrusher. The other cases are unlocked however.

You will still have to fight the Ash Zombies and if you return to Ashfall Tear after that, you will find the Reclamation Priest with three Redoran Guards investigating the scene while sadly saying "Almsivi" to themselves. They will ask what you want but no dialogue will be available.

You will have all four masks, not replicas, but they have no associated magical qualities.

## Notes

- Disposition with heretics can be elevated in 3 ways, either finishing three tasks, or combating against 4 potential followers, or persuading Matriarch Drevlan and receiving Almalexia blessing, followers will become available as soon as their disposition toward you are elevated.
- 3 ways above can lead to complete "(Optional) Earn the Matriarch's trust and join the temple heretics", then you can equip whatever armor instead of [Kenro's Helmet and Robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_Items#Unique_Apparel "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal Items")

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccASVSSE001_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccASVSSE001_Quest`.

# Skyrim:Giant Camps

## Overview

Talking Stone Camp

 This page lists all the **giant camps** in [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim"). [Military camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps") are listed on a separate page, as are bandit and [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") [camps](/wiki/Skyrim:Camps "Skyrim:Camps"); these other types of camps use different map marker icons.

:    **[Bleakwind Basin](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleakwind_Basin "Skyrim:Bleakwind Basin")** — A giant camp west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bleakwind+Basin)
:    **[Blizzard Rest](/wiki/Skyrim:Blizzard_Rest "Skyrim:Blizzard Rest")** — A giant camp south of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Blizzard+Rest)
:    **[Broken Limb Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Limb_Camp "Skyrim:Broken Limb Camp")** — A giant camp north-northwest of Darkwater Crossing. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Broken+Limb+Camp)
:    **[Cradlecrush Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Cradlecrush_Rock "Skyrim:Cradlecrush Rock")** — A giant camp southwest of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Cradlecrush+Rock)
:    **[Guldun Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Guldun_Rock "Skyrim:Guldun Rock")** — A giant camp east of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Guldun+Rock)
:    **[Red Road Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Road_Pass "Skyrim:Red Road Pass")** — A giant camp south-southwest of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Red+Road+Pass)
:    **[Secunda's Kiss](/wiki/Skyrim:Secunda%27s_Kiss "Skyrim:Secunda's Kiss")** — A giant camp southwest of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Secunda%27s+Kiss)
:    **[Sleeping Tree Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Tree_Camp "Skyrim:Sleeping Tree Camp")** — A giant camp west of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Sleeping+Tree+Camp)
:    **[Steamcrag Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Steamcrag_Camp "Skyrim:Steamcrag Camp")** — A giant camp south of Windhelm. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Steamcrag+Camp)
:    **[Stonehill Bluff](/wiki/Skyrim:Stonehill_Bluff "Skyrim:Stonehill Bluff")** — A giant camp south-southwest of Dawnstar. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Stonehill+Bluff)
:    **[Talking Stone Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Talking_Stone_Camp "Skyrim:Talking Stone Camp")** — A giant camp northeast of Rorikstead. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Talking+Stone+Camp)
:    **[Tumble Arch Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Tumble_Arch_Pass "Skyrim:Tumble Arch Pass")** — A giant camp northeast of Whiterun. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Tumble+Arch+Pass)

# Skyrim:Giant's Grove

## Overview

Giant's Grove

**Giant's Grove** is a grove accessed through [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave") containing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") whose tribe has defiled a shrine of [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

Shrine of Malacath

The giants attack the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") due to the curse bestowed on them by the Daedric Prince. The grove is inaccessible until the quest [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") has been started.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

## Walkthrough

Corpses encircle a massive bonfire in front of the gory shrine of Malacath. A boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on the ground are near the base of the shrine. Four [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") are also in the vicinity: two are on the ground next to the wall (with one east of the bonfire and the other to the west), the third is south of the shrine, and the fourth is directly behind the shrine. The hostile unnamed giant will attack you on sight and carries the quest-related weapon [Shagrol's Warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Shagrol%27s_Warhammer "Skyrim:Shagrol's Warhammer").

## Notes

- You cannot wait in this location.
- The burnt body on a pole at the campfire cannot be eaten if you activate [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form").
- You can fast travel *to* this location, but not *from* this location. To exit, you'll have to backtrack through Fallowstone Cave. You can fast travel again once you exit the cave via the main entrance.
- This location is one of the easternmost locations in the game you can visit.
- This location cannot be independently [cleared](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons"). It will only display as cleared when the boss-level creatures in Fallowstone Cave have been killed, as the game considers these two zones as one unit for this purpose. As a result, Giant's Grove itself will never be added to your count of cleared locations, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.

## Bugs

- A Mammoth Cheese sack may appear embedded into the ground near statue of Malacath, and a giant's club may clip through the ground near there.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

Giant's Grove

**Giant's Grove** is a grove accessed through [Fallowstone Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Fallowstone_Cave "Skyrim:Fallowstone Cave") containing a [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") whose tribe has defiled a shrine of [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

Shrine of Malacath

The giants attack the [Orc stronghold](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc_Strongholds "Skyrim:Orc Strongholds") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") due to the curse bestowed on them by the Daedric Prince. The grove is inaccessible until the quest [The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe") has been started.

## Related Quests

- **[The Cursed Tribe](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Cursed_Tribe "Skyrim:The Cursed Tribe")**: Help lift the curse placed on the [Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") of [Largashbur](/wiki/Skyrim:Largashbur "Skyrim:Largashbur") by [Malacath](/wiki/Lore:Malacath "Lore:Malacath").

## Walkthrough

Corpses encircle a massive bonfire in front of the gory shrine of Malacath. A boss [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") on the ground are near the base of the shrine. Four [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") are also in the vicinity: two are on the ground next to the wall (with one east of the bonfire and the other to the west), the third is south of the shrine, and the fourth is directly behind the shrine. The hostile unnamed giant will attack you on sight and carries the quest-related weapon [Shagrol's Warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Shagrol%27s_Warhammer "Skyrim:Shagrol's Warhammer").

## Notes

- You cannot wait in this location.
- The burnt body on a pole at the campfire cannot be eaten if you activate [Beast Form](/wiki/Skyrim:Beast_Form "Skyrim:Beast Form").
- You can fast travel *to* this location, but not *from* this location. To exit, you'll have to backtrack through Fallowstone Cave. You can fast travel again once you exit the cave via the main entrance.
- This location is one of the easternmost locations in the game you can visit.
- This location cannot be independently [cleared](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons"). It will only display as cleared when the boss-level creatures in Fallowstone Cave have been killed, as the game considers these two zones as one unit for this purpose. As a result, Giant's Grove itself will never be added to your count of cleared locations, and therefore does not contribute to the [Delver](/wiki/Skyrim:Delver "Skyrim:Delver") achievement.

## Bugs

- A Mammoth Cheese sack may appear embedded into the ground near statue of Malacath, and a giant's club may clip through the ground near there.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Giant's Tooth

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Worldspace: Giant's Tooth ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Giant%27s+Tooth+%28CC%29)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Giant%27s_Tooth "Lore:Giant's Tooth")) | | |

| Occupants | |
| [Giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant"), [Ice Wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"). [Rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit"), [Snow Foxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Fox "Skyrim:Snow Fox") | |

| Far northeast of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") | |
| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Giant's Tooth

**Giant's Tooth** is a small island in the [Sea of Ghosts](/wiki/Skyrim:Sea_of_Ghosts "Skyrim:Sea of Ghosts"). It can only be reached by speaking to the [ferryman](/wiki/Skyrim:Ferryman "Skyrim:Ferryman") [Harlaug](/wiki/Skyrim:Harlaug "Skyrim:Harlaug") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") during the quest [A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish").

The island consists of a small [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") and the entrance to [Iron Tusk Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Tusk_Cave "Skyrim:Iron Tusk Cave"). You will be sent here to retrieve an [Ironwood Fruit](/wiki/Skyrim:Ironwood_Fruit "Skyrim:Ironwood Fruit") during the related quest, although these six rare trees only grow in the conditions inside the cave.

The camp is populated by two [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") and contains two dead [mammoths](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth "Skyrim:Mammoth"). [Snow foxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox "Skyrim:Fox") will also spawn around the camp and inside the cave. Upon approaching the Ironwood Fruit trees inside the cave, three [spriggans](/wiki/Skyrim:Spriggan "Skyrim:Spriggan") will awaken and attack you. Live [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") can be found on the island's shoreline. When you exit the cave after retrieving the Ironwood Fruit, three [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith") will appear and attack you. A *[Fisherman's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman%27s_Note "Skyrim:Fisherman's Note")* can be found on a chopping block in the camp.

## Related Quests

- **[A Dying Wish](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dying_Wish "Skyrim:A Dying Wish")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup"): Make a bitter choice.

## Notes

- Although this location has a [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") map marker, it cannot be fast traveled to from mainland [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim_(place) "Skyrim:Skyrim (place)").
- It is not possible to swim around the island or climb over the mountains to the other side. Using TCL shows that the backside of the island is unfinished in design.
- [Nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") can be found on the outskirts of the location by the western shoreline and inside the cave.
- An [Iron Ore](/wiki/Online:Iron_Ore "Online:Iron Ore") vein can be found on the north side of the cave entrance.
- Two [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") can be found in the raft right next to Harlaug's.

# Skyrim:Gift of Kynareth

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This page is currently being rewritten as part of the [Skyrim Quest Redesign Project](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").** The page is being rewritten and checked in several stages. All users are welcome to make changes to the page. If you make a change that is relevant to the project, please update this template accordingly, and make sure you have observed the [project guidelines](/wiki/UESPWiki:Skyrim_Quest_Redesign_Project#Guidelines "UESPWiki:Skyrim Quest Redesign Project").  Details  **Walkthrough**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), *not checked*  **Reward**: written by [Legoless](/wiki/User:Legoless "User:Legoless"), checked by [Dillonn241](/wiki/User:Dillonn241 "User:Dillonn241") |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Recover a legendary [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") [artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") and obtain the blessing of [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | Reading the [letter to General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_General_Tullius "Skyrim:Letter to General Tullius") |
| Location(s): | [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour"), camp southeast of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor"), [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") |
| Reward: | [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE021\_LordsMailQuest |
| Added by: | [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail "Skyrim:Lord's Mail") |

Alik'r mercenaries have stolen the Armor of [Morihaus](/wiki/Lore:Morihaus "Lore:Morihaus")

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Travel to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") and read the Emperor's [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_General_Tullius "Skyrim:Letter to General Tullius").
2. Locate the camp southeast of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") and defeat the [Alik'r mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Mercenary "Skyrim:Alik'r Mercenary").
3. Take the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alik%27r_Mercenary_Chest "Skyrim:Key to Alik'r Mercenary Chest") from [Majid](/wiki/Skyrim:Majid_the_Mad "Skyrim:Majid the Mad") and recover the [cursed Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(Cursed) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (Cursed)").
4. Go to Kynareth's shrine at the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") to claim the [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)").

### Mission from the Emperor

The letter in Castle Dour

Head to [Castle Dour](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Dour "Skyrim:Castle Dour") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") to intercept a letter from the Emperor. The [*Letter to General Tullius*](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_to_General_Tullius "Skyrim:Letter to General Tullius") can be found on the ground floor of Castle Dour in the room to the north of [General Tullius's](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") map room. You are only required to read the letter to start the quest; taking it counts as theft, so be sure that you are not seen if you decide to take it with you. The letter reveals that the [Lord's Mail](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(item) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (item)"), a legendary [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") artifact, has been stolen by a band of [Alik'r mercenaries](/wiki/Skyrim:Alik%27r_Mercenary "Skyrim:Alik'r Mercenary") who were last seen south of [Fort Greymoor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greymoor "Skyrim:Fort Greymoor") in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold").

The Alik'r camp is actually located southeast of Fort Greymoor, and is home to two generic Alik'r mercenaries led by [Majid the Mad](/wiki/Skyrim:Majid_the_Mad "Skyrim:Majid the Mad"). Taking on all three at once can be a tough fight, so prepare accordingly. Once the mercenaries lie dead, recover the [Key to Alik'r Mercenary Chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Alik%27r_Mercenary_Chest "Skyrim:Key to Alik'r Mercenary Chest") from Majid's body and use it to open the nearby chest. Inside, you will find a [cursed version](/wiki/Skyrim:Lord%27s_Mail_(Cursed) "Skyrim:Lord's Mail (Cursed)") of the Lord's Mail along with a set of instructions titled *[Majid - Please Read](/wiki/Skyrim:Majid_-_Please_Read "Skyrim:Majid - Please Read")*. The note warns that the cursed armor should not be worn; indeed, if you equip it you will be subjected to a constant 50-point reduction to your Health, Stamina, and Magicka.

### Blessing of Kynareth

In order to remove the curse from the Lord's Mail, you will need to seek the blessing of its mythic creator, [Kynareth](/wiki/Lore:Kynareth "Lore:Kynareth"). This will necessitate a return to Solitude to visit the [Shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth") in the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines"). Upon activating the shrine, you will be informed that *"The Lord's Mail has been cleansed"*. This concludes the quest and rewards you with a set of [heavy](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor_(item) "Skyrim:Heavy Armor (item)") [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") armor with [poison resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Poison "Skyrim:Resist Poison"), [magic resistance](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Magic "Skyrim:Resist Magic"), as well as a unique area effect that inflicts 5 points of [health absorbance](/wiki/Skyrim:Absorb_Health "Skyrim:Absorb Health") per second on nearby opponents. For the purpose of the [*Matching Set*](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor#Matching_Set "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") perk, it counts as [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor#Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor").

## Notes

- For historical information on the Lord's Mail, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Lord%27s_Mail "Lore:Lord's Mail").
- The Alik'r mercenaries wear unique Redguard clothing items.
- If playing on Survival Mode, you will need to disable Survival Mode in order to complete the quest and get the Lord's Mail. The easiest way is to disable Survival mode outside of the temple then re-enable it once you've cleansed the armor. For some reason, it won't work when you have to pay to use the shrine.

## Quest Stages

| Gift of Kynareth (ccBGSSSE021\_LordsMailQuest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 0 |  | A letter from the Emperor pertaining to an Imperial artifact was found at Castle Dour. I should read it and find out what it's about. *Objective :* Read the Emperor's Letter |
| 10 |  | I've found a letter addressed to General Tullius from the Emperor of Tamriel instructing that The Lord's Mail, a treasured Imperial relic, be found and reclaimed. A band of Redguard mercenaries are rumored to have taken it. I should locate their whereabouts and see if I can obtain the artifact. *Objective :* Confront the Alik'r Mercenaries |
| 15 |  | I've confronted the Alik'r mercenaries and found a locked chest. I just need to find the key... *Objective :* Retrieve the Lord's Mail |
| 20 |  | I've retrieved The Lord's Mail, the legendary Imperial armor. Before it can be worn, it must be cleansed at the shrine of Kynareth in Solitude. *Objective :* Cleanse the Lord's Mail in Solitude |
| 30 | ☑ | The Lord's Mail has been retrieved, blessed by Kynareth, and can now be worn safely. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE021_LordsMailQuest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE021_LordsMailQuest`.

# Skyrim:Gilfre's House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Gilfre's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gilfre%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| MixwaterMillGilfresHouse | |
| Location | |
| [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |
| # of [Wood Chopping Blocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Chop_Wood "Skyrim:Chop Wood") | 1 |

Gilfre's House next to Mixwater Mill

**Gilfre's House** is the home owned by [Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") at [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill").

Located southeast of [Gallows Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallows_Rock "Skyrim:Gallows Rock") and southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), [Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") has lived here alone since her five workers left to fight in the civil war.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Gilfre](/wiki/Skyrim:Gilfre "Skyrim:Gilfre") |

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

It is on the banks of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), which is used to power the mill via a water wheel. The house, a [worker's house](/wiki/Skyrim:Worker%27s_House "Skyrim:Worker's House") and the sawmill itself are all part of [Mixwater Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Mixwater_Mill "Skyrim:Mixwater Mill"). Everything on the deck in front of the house is owned and taking anything is considered stealing, though there is a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") that you can take for free. There is a rack holding four [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") and a crate with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack on top and the aforementioned woodcutter's axe leaning against it. There is a chicken coop with three [nests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") for the four [chickens](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken") that wander the site between this and the worker's house. Also there are several [blue](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower") and [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") and at least one [snowberry bush](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") around the house and site. On the bank by the sawmill is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"). The front door is novice-locked most of the day and all night.

### Gilfre's House

Gilfre's bedroom

It is a single-roomed dwelling containing a double bed coming out from the east wall, with a set of shelves to the left, against the north wall. These hold six common books, two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") and several [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), with several pieces of cheese and a plate containing two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") on top. Hanging from the ceiling above the shelves are two garlic braids, three bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). To the left of the shelves is a flower basket containing three [chicken's eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and to the right is a food barrel. There is an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed and to the right, against the south wall is a round wooden table with two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") on top, while next to the table is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"). To the right of this is a rack hanging from the ceiling holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)").

Opposite the entrance is a fireplace, on the south wall, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging in front and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes "Skyrim:Shoes") by the hearth. There are eight loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on the mantelpiece. To the right of the fireplace, also against the south wall is a long wooden table and bench, with two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a sprig of snowberries, a [salmon steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a potato, a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), several loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top of the table, with a [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor") on the floor underneath. In the northeastern corner is a square wooden table and two chairs. On this table is a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Marksmanship Lesson](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Marksmanship_Lesson "Skyrim:The Marksmanship Lesson")*, a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a random [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") potion and five loose septims.

## Notes

- You may choose to live here if you [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") Gilfe. Like at [Volkihar Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Keep "Skyrim:Volkihar Keep") and [Fort Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Fort Dawnguard") after completing [Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline") quest, everything on the deck in front of the house except for the woodcutter's axe will still be owned, though, and must be stolen.

## Bugs

- If you marry Gilfre, sleeping in the bed in her house only confers a Rested bonus, not Lover's Comfort or Well-Rested. **?**
- If you move here after marrying Gilfre, she may still ask you to leave.

# Skyrim:Gjukar's Monument

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Landmark.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Landmark.png) | Landmark: Gjukar's Monument ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Gjukar%27s+Monument)) | | |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 12 |

Gjukar's Monument

**Gjukar's Monument** is a stone monument commemorating an ancient battle southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead").

A sword, a shield, and a few flowers are at the base of the monument. During the quest [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love"), a ghost named [Ruki](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruki "Skyrim:Ruki") can be found here searching for her husband [Fenrig](/wiki/Skyrim:Fenrig "Skyrim:Fenrig").

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.

## Notes

- An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is near the road south of the monument.
- A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is among the rocks north of the monument.
- Due east of the monument is an [unmarked ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Crumbling_Bastion "Skyrim:Shrines") containing a [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar"), an [amulet of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Amulet of Zenithar"), a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")*, two [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), with a novice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") directly above these items on top of the ruin.
- Southeast of the monument near the road is a pool with the remains of a long-dead colossal [mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab "Skyrim:Mudcrab") surrounded by its smaller living cousins. These remains will be joined by the [Mudcrab Guardian Spirit](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Guardian_Spirit "Skyrim:Mudcrab Guardian Spirit") during the quest [Kyne's Sacred Trials](/wiki/Skyrim:Kyne%27s_Sacred_Trials "Skyrim:Kyne's Sacred Trials").

Glacial Cave

**Glacial Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Benkongerike](/wiki/Skyrim:Benkongerike "Skyrim:Benkongerike") containing [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). It contains only one zone, *[Glacial Cave](#Glacial_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").
- **[Summoning Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Summoning_Karstaag "Skyrim:Summoning Karstaag")**: Summon and defeat [Karstaag](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag "Skyrim:Karstaag").

### Exterior

On either side of the entrance are barrels and crates, including a fish barrel and a food barrel. On the left, partially buried in the snow between two crates, is an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") containing an [East Empire pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") and other loot. Along the cliff face to the right is a [malachite ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Malachite Ore Vein") and six [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants yielding [ashen grass pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashen_Grass_Pod "Skyrim:Ashen Grass Pod"), while a [nirnroot](/wiki/Skyrim:Nirnroot "Skyrim:Nirnroot") plant and two [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") are along the shore. Two horkers are just northeast of the entrance.

### Glacial Cave

Upon entering, an icy tunnel descends to the southeast, with rocks and fencing made from [rieklings spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Spear "Skyrim:Riekling Spear") on either side. By the second set of fencing is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on top of a crate. The tunnel bears to the south, then turns back to the southeast by two barrels. The passage soon opens into a cavern, with a riekling tent on the far side, and barrels and crates along the walls at the end of the tunnel and in the cavern.

As you enter the cavern, you are at the top of some shallow ledges above the cavern floor. There are three rieklings waiting to ambush you beneath the snow. Use of the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") will reveal them to you. As you move forward, they will burst from the snow and attack. On your right is an ice pillar with a [riekling hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut") behind it. Against the northeast wall on the ground is a malachite ore vein. To the right of the vein is the tent seen from the tunnel, with an open crate containing a goblet inside. At the back of the cave, wedged into a crack on the wall, is [Karstaag's skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Karstaag%27s_Skull "Skyrim:Karstaag's Skull").

## Notes

- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up fully, unlike most interior locations, although it is still warmer than outside.
